TL;DR: 本文提出了Omni-Masked Gradient Descent (OMGD)，一种基于掩码遍历的内存高效优化方法。该方法在非凸设置下实现了$\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(\varepsilon^{-3})$的迭代复杂度，相比标准的$\mathcal{O}(\varepsilon^{-4})$有严格改进，并且可以无缝集成到主流优化器中，在微调和预训练任务上均表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模语言模型的参数训练受到GPU内存瓶颈的限制。现有的内存高效优化方法要么缺乏清晰的收敛保证，要么在非凸设置下仅能达到标准的$\mathcal{O}(\varepsilon^{-4})$迭代复杂度，需要一种既有理论保证又有更好收敛性的方法。

Method: 提出了Omni-Masked Gradient Descent (OMGD)，一种基于掩码遍历的内存高效训练方法。该方法是一个轻量级、即插即用的方法，可以无缝集成到大多数主流优化器中，并提供了非凸收敛分析。

Result: 在非凸设置下建立了严格改进的迭代复杂度$\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(\varepsilon^{-3})$，用于寻找$\varepsilon$近似驻点，这比标准的$\mathcal{O}(\varepsilon^{-4})$复杂度有显著提升。在微调和预训练任务的实验中，OMGD在竞争基线上取得了一致的改进效果。

Conclusion: OMGD成功地在保证理论收敛性的前提下，实现了更好的迭代复杂度和内存效率，同时具有良好的实用性和兼容性，为大规模语言模型的高效训练提供了一种有效的解决方案。

Abstract: Memory-efficient optimization methods have recently gained increasing attention for scaling full-parameter training of large language models under the GPU-memory bottleneck. Existing approaches either lack clear convergence guarantees, or only achieve the standard ${\mathcal{O}}(ε^{-4})$ iteration complexity in the nonconvex settings. We propose Omni-Masked Gradient Descent (OMGD), an optimization method based on mask traversal for memory efficient training, and provide a nonconvex convergence analysis that establishes a strictly improved iteration complexity of $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(ε^{-3})$ for finding an $ε$-approximate stationary point. Empirically, OMGD is a lightweight, plug-and-play approach that integrates seamlessly into most mainstream optimizers, yielding consistent improvements over competitive baselines in both fine-tuning and pre-training tasks.

### [101] [EvoESAP: Non-Uniform Expert Pruning for Sparse MoE](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06003)
*Zongfang Liu,Shengkun Tang,Boyang Sun,Zhiqiang Shen,Xin Yuan*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对稀疏混合专家语言模型的专家剪枝方法。通过引入预期推测接受代理(ESAP)指标来评估剪枝模型的质量，并基于此开发了EvoESAP进化搜索框架，用于优化非均匀层级稀疏分配。实验表明，在相同稀疏度下，该方法在开放生成任务上相比均匀剪枝提升了最高19.6%的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有SMoE模型的部署受限于内存和吞吐量，因为需要存储和提供完整的专家池。现有的后训练专家剪枝方法主要关注每层内剪枝哪些专家，但默认采用均匀的层级稀疏分配，而忽略了非均匀分配对性能的潜在影响。

Method: 本文将剪枝解耦为层内专家排序和跨层预算分配两个步骤。首先提出ESAP(预期推测接受代理)，这是一种受推测解码启发的教师强制指标，用于衡量剪枝模型与完整模型的匹配程度。ESAP具有有界性和稳定性，能够低成本地比较大量候选方案。在此基础上，提出EvoESAP进化搜索框架，在固定全局预算下优化非均匀层级稀疏分配，同时保持层内剪枝顺序不变，可与Frequency、EAN、SEER、REAP等现有标准结合使用。

Result: 在7B-30B规模的SMoE大语言模型上，分别在25%和50%稀疏度下进行测试。EvoESAP持续发现能够改善开放生成性能的非均匀分配方案，在MATH-500数据集上50%稀疏度时性能提升高达19.6%，同时在多项选择准确率上保持与均匀剪枝相当的竞争力。

Conclusion: 通过解耦剪枝过程并引入ESAP评估指标，本文证明了非均匀层级稀疏分配相比传统均匀分配具有显著优势。EvoESAP框架作为一个即插即用的方法，能够与多种现有剪枝标准结合，在保持计算效率的同时显著提升SMoE模型的剪枝性能。

Abstract: Sparse Mixture-of-Experts (SMoE) language models achieve strong capability at low per-token compute, yet deployment remains memory- and throughput-bound because the full expert pool must be stored and served. Post-training expert pruning reduces this cost, but most methods focus on which experts to prune within each layer and default to a uniform layer-wise sparsity allocation, even though the allocation can strongly affect performance. We decouple pruning into within-layer expert ranking and across-layer budget allocation, and introduce \textbf{E}xpected \textbf{S}peculative \textbf{A}cceptance \textbf{P}roxy (\textbf{ESAP}), a speculative-decoding-inspired, teacher-forced metric that measures how well a pruned model matches the full model. ESAP is bounded and stable, enabling cheap comparison of many candidates without costly autoregressive decoding. Building on ESAP, we propose EvoESAP, an evolutionary searching framework that optimizes a non-uniform layer-wise sparsity allocation under a fixed global budget while holding the within-layer pruning order fixed, making it a plug-and-play method with criteria such as Frequency, EAN, SEER, and REAP. Across 7B--30B SMoE LLMs at 25\% and 50\% sparsity, EvoESAP consistently discovers non-uniform allocations that improve open-ended generation (up to \textbf{+19.6\%} on MATH-500 at 50\% sparsity) while preserving competitive multiple-choice accuracy compared with uniform pruning at the same sparsity.

### [102] [Preventing Learning Stagnation in PPO by Scaling to 1 Million Parallel Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06009)
*Michael Beukman,Khimya Khetarpal,Zeyu Zheng,Will Dabney,Jakob Foerster,Michael Dennis,Clare Lyle*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了PPO算法中性能停滞于次优水平的一种新原因：外层循环步长相对于噪声过大，并提出了通过大规模并行化（扩展至100万以上环境）来解决该问题的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在深度同策略强化学习（特别是PPO）中，智能体性能常在次优水平停滞（plateaus）。现有研究将其归因于探索不足、容量限制或优化困难，但本文发现某些情况下的停滞源于：基于样本的损失估计在训练过程中逐渐偏离真实目标函数。这一发现促使作者重新审视PPO的外层循环机制。

Method: 将PPO的外层循环（策略采样）建模为随机优化问题，其中步长由正则化强度控制，梯度噪声由两次更新间收集的样本数决定。模型预测：当外层步长相对于噪声过大时，性能会停滞于次优水平。基于此，提出两种解决方案：减小步长或增加更新间的样本数。作者系统研究了超参数如何影响步长和更新噪声，发现增加并行环境数是降低两者的简单稳健方法，并提出了一套超参数协同扩展方案。

Result: 1. 模型预测得到实验验证；2. 增加并行环境数能有效降低步长和噪声；3. 提出了超参数协同扩展方案，并证明错误的扩展会导致严重的性能下降；4. 通过将PPO扩展至超过100万个并行环境，在复杂开放域中大幅超越先前基线，实现了在1万亿转移步骤内的单调性能提升。

Conclusion: PPO性能停滞的核心原因在于外层循环的步长与噪声不匹配，而非传统的探索或优化问题。通过大规模并行化（100万+环境）并正确协同扩展超参数，可以解决学习停滞问题，实现单调性能提升。这为大规模强化学习系统提供了重要的理论和实践指导。

Abstract: Plateaus, where an agent's performance stagnates at a suboptimal level, are a common problem in deep on-policy RL. Focusing on PPO due to its widespread adoption, we show that plateaus in certain regimes arise not because of known exploration, capacity, or optimization challenges, but because sample-based estimates of the loss eventually become poor proxies for the true objective over the course of training. As a recap, PPO switches between sampling rollouts from several parallel environments online using the current policy (which we call the outer loop) and performing repeated minibatch SGD steps against this offline dataset (the inner loop). In our work we consider only the outer loop, and conceptually model it as stochastic optimization. The step size is then controlled by the regularization strength towards the previous policy and the gradient noise by the number of samples collected between policy update steps. This model predicts that performance will plateau at a suboptimal level if the outer step size is too large relative to the noise. Recasting PPO in this light makes it clear that there are two ways to address this particular type of learning stagnation: either reduce the step size or increase the number of samples collected between updates. We first validate the predictions of our model and investigate how hyperparameter choices influence the step size and update noise, concluding that increasing the number of parallel environments is a simple and robust way to reduce both factors. Next, we propose a recipe for how to co-scale the other hyperparameters when increasing parallelization, and show that incorrectly doing so can lead to severe performance degradation. Finally, we vastly outperform prior baselines in a complex open-ended domain by scaling PPO to more than 1M parallel environments, thereby enabling monotonic performance improvement up to one trillion transitions.

</details>


### [103] [Agnostic learning in (almost) optimal time via Gaussian surface area](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06027)

Abstract: The complexity of learning a concept class under Gaussian marginals in the difficult agnostic model is closely related to its $L_1$-approximability by low-degree polynomials. For any concept class with Gaussian surface area at most $Γ$, Klivans et al. (2008) show that degree $d = O(Γ^2 / \varepsilon^4)$ suffices to achieve an $\varepsilon$-approximation. This leads to the best-known bounds on the complexity of learning a variety of concept classes. In this note, we improve their analysis by showing that degree $d = \tilde O (Γ^2 / \varepsilon^2)$ is enough. In light of lower bounds due to Diakonikolas et al. (2021), this yields (near) optimal bounds on the complexity of agnostically learning polynomial threshold functions in the statistical query model. Our proof relies on a direct analogue of a construction of Feldman et al. (2020), who considered $L_1$-approximation on the Boolean hypercube.

### [105] [Improved high-dimensional estimation with Langevin dynamics and stochastic weight averaging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06028)
*Stanley Wei,Alex Damian,Jason D. Lee*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文证明了通过使用迭代平均而非最终迭代，Langevin动力学可以在$n \gtrsim d^{k^\star/2}$样本下恢复隐藏方向，无需显式平滑，噪声注入与迭代平均的结合能够模拟景观平滑的效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究表明，在线SGD和Langevin动力学恢复隐藏 planted 方向$\theta^\star$需要$n \gtrsim d^{\max(1, k^\star-1)}$样本，其中$k^\star$是信息指数。Damian等人(2023)证明在平滑景观上运行梯度下降可以用$n \gtrsim d^{\max(1, k^\star/2)}$样本成功，这引发了是否能在无显式平滑的情况下达到相同速率的问题。

Method: 作者研究Langevin动力学，但考虑平均迭代而非最终迭代。核心思想是噪声注入与迭代平均的结合能够模拟景观平滑的效果，从而避免显式平滑操作。该方法应用于张量PCA和单索引模型两种设置。

Result: 证明了Langevin动力学配合迭代平均可以在$n \gtrsim d^{k^\star/2}$样本下成功恢复隐藏方向$\theta^\star$，达到了与显式平滑方法相同的样本复杂度，且无需额外的平滑操作。

Conclusion: 通过噪声注入和迭代平均的组合，Langevin动力学能够隐式地实现景观平滑的效果，从而突破了原有下界限制。作者还推测minibatch SGD无需添加额外噪声也能达到相同速率。

Abstract: Significant recent work has studied the ability of gradient descent to recover a hidden planted direction $θ^\star \in S^{d-1}$ in different high-dimensional settings, including tensor PCA and single-index models. The key quantity that governs the ability of gradient descent to traverse these landscapes is the information exponent $k^\star$ (Ben Arous et al., (2021)), which corresponds to the order of the saddle at initialization in the population landscape. Ben Arous et al., (2021) showed that $n \gtrsim d^{\max(1, k^\star-1)}$ samples were necessary and sufficient for online SGD to recover $θ^\star$, and Ben Arous et al., (2020) proved a similar lower bound for Langevin dynamics. More recently, Damian et al., (2023) showed it was possible to circumvent these lower bounds by running gradient descent on a smoothed landscape, and that this algorithm succeeds with $n \gtrsim d^{\max(1, k^\star/2)}$ samples, which is optimal in the worst case. This raises the question of whether it is possible to achieve the same rate without explicit smoothing. In this paper, we show that Langevin dynamics can succeed with $n \gtrsim d^{ k^\star/2 }$ samples if one considers the average iterate, rather than the last iterate. The key idea is that the combination of noise-injection and iterate averaging is able to emulate the effect of landscape smoothing. We apply this result to both the tensor PCA and single-index model settings. Finally, we conjecture that minibatch SGD can also achieve the same rate without adding any additional noise.

  <summary>Details</summary>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Current approaches fail to develop an efficient solver for this orienteering problem variant with discrete and continuous variables. In this paper, we propose a learning-based two-stage DEcoupled discrete-Continuous optimization with Service-time-guided Trajectory (DeCoST), which aims to effectively decouple the discrete and continuous decision variables in the OPTWVP problem, while enabling efficient and learnable coordination between them. In the first stage, a parallel decoding structure is employed to predict the path and the initial service time allocation. The second stage optimizes the service times through a linear programming (LP) formulation and provides a long-horizon learning of structure estimation. We rigorously prove the global optimality of the second-stage solution. Experiments on OPTWVP instances demonstrate that DeCoST outperforms both state-of-the-art constructive solvers and the latest meta-heuristic algorithms in terms of solution quality and computational efficiency, achieving up to 6.6x inference speedup on instances with fewer than 500 nodes. ### [111] [DQE: A Semantic-Aware Evaluation Metric for Time Series Anomaly Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06131)
*Yuewei Li,Dalin Zhang,Huan Li,Xinyi Gong,Hongjun Chu,Zhaohui Song*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对时间序列异常检测中现有评估指标的局限性，提出了一种基于检测语义的新评估指标，通过分区策略和全阈值谱聚合方法实现了更稳定、更具区分性和可解释性的评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有时间序列异常检测评估指标存在四个主要局限：偏向点级覆盖率、对近似缺失检测不敏感或不一致、对误报警惩罚不足、以及阈值选择导致的不一致性，这些问题会产生不可靠或违反直觉的结果，阻碍客观进展。

Method: 提出基于检测语义的分区策略，将每个异常的局部时间区域分解为三个功能不同的子区域；在此基础上设计细粒度评分机制评估各子区域；识别阈值区间选择相关的评估偏差，采用全阈值谱聚合检测质量的方法消除评估不一致性。

Result: 在合成数据和真实数据上的大量实验表明，该指标相比十种广泛使用的指标，能够提供稳定、具区分性和可解释的评估，并实现稳健的评估效果。

Conclusion: 所提出的评估指标有效解决了现有指标的局限性，为时间序列异常检测提供了更可靠、一致且可解释的评估框架，有助于推动该领域的客观发展。

Abstract: Time series anomaly detection has achieved remarkable progress in recent years. However, evaluation practices have received comparatively less attention, despite their critical importance. Existing metrics exhibit several limitations: (1) bias toward point-level coverage, (2) insensitivity or inconsistency in near-miss detections, (3) inadequate penalization of false alarms, and (4) inconsistency caused by threshold or threshold-interval selection. These limitations can produce unreliable or counterintuitive results, hindering objective progress. In this work, we revisit the evaluation of time series anomaly detection from the perspective of detection semantics and propose a novel metric for more comprehensive assessment. We first introduce a partitioning strategy grounded in detection semantics, which decomposes the local temporal region of each anomaly into three functionally distinct subregions. Using this partitioning, we evaluate overall detection behavior across events and design finer-grained scoring mechanisms for each subregion, enabling more reliable and interpretable assessment. Through a systematic study of existing metrics, we identify an evaluation bias associated with threshold-interval selection and adopt an approach that aggregates detection qualities across the full threshold spectrum, thereby eliminating evaluation inconsistency. Extensive experiments on synthetic and real-world data demonstrate that our metric provides stable, discriminative, and interpretable evaluation, while achieving robust assessment compared with ten widely used metrics.

### [112] [Agentic retrieval-augmented reasoning reshapes collective reliability under model variability in radiology question answering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06271)
*Mina Farajiamiri,Jeta Sopa,Saba Afza,Lisa Adams,Felix Barajas Ordonez,Tri-Thien Nguyen,Mahshad Lotfinia,Sebastian Wind,Keno Bressem,Sven Nebelung,Daniel Truhn,Soroosh Tayebi Arasteh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究评估了代理检索增强推理（agentic retrieval-augmented reasoning）对34个大语言模型在放射学问答任务中的可靠性影响，发现该方法显著降低了模型间决策分歧、增强了共识强度和正确性的跨模型稳健性，但仅靠准确率或一致性评估不足以全面表征系统可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管代理检索增强推理管道在临床决策支持中应用日益广泛，但其对模型变异性下可靠性的影响尚不明确。现实中异构模型可能以准确率无法捕捉的方式出现对齐、分歧或同步错误，因此需要深入研究此类系统对模型间决策一致性和稳健性的影响。

Method: 研究者在169个专家策划的放射学公开问答数据集上评估了34个大语言模型，比较了零样本推理与放射学专用多步代理检索条件。在代理检索条件下，所有模型均接收来自策划放射学知识的相同结构化证据报告，从而系统性地对比两种推理策略的效果。

Result: 代理推理显著降低了模型间决策分歧（中位熵值从0.48降至0.13），提高了跨模型正确性的稳健性（均值从0.74升至0.81），并增强了多数共识（P<0.001）。共识强度与稳健正确性在两种策略下均保持相关（零样本ρ=0.88，代理ρ=0.87），但高一致性并不保证正确性。在572个错误输出中，72%与中度或高度临床严重性相关。

Conclusion: 代理检索增强推理与更集中的决策分布、更强的共识和更高的跨模型正确性稳健性相关。研究结果表明，仅通过准确率或一致性评估代理系统可能不足，需要补充分析稳定性、跨模型稳健性和潜在临床影响，以全面表征模型变异性下的可靠性。

Abstract: Agentic retrieval-augmented reasoning pipelines are increasingly used to structure how large language models (LLMs) incorporate external evidence in clinical decision support. These systems iteratively retrieve curated domain knowledge and synthesize it into structured reports before answer selection. Although such pipelines can improve performance, their impact on reliability under model variability remains unclear. In real-world deployment, heterogeneous models may align, diverge, or synchronize errors in ways not captured by accuracy. We evaluated 34 LLMs on 169 expert-curated publicly available radiology questions, comparing zero-shot inference with a radiology-specific multi-step agentic retrieval condition in which all models received identical structured evidence reports derived from curated radiology knowledge. Agentic inference reduced inter-model decision dispersion (median entropy 0.48 vs. 0.13) and increased robustness of correctness across models (mean 0.74 vs. 0.81). Majority consensus also increased overall (P<0.001). Consensus strength and robust correctness remained correlated under both strategies (\r{ho}=0.88 for zero-shot; \r{ho}=0.87 for agentic), although high agreement did not guarantee correctness. Response verbosity showed no meaningful association with correctness. Among 572 incorrect outputs, 72% were associated with moderate or high clinically assessed severity, although inter-rater agreement was low (\k{appa}=0.02). Agentic retrieval therefore was associated with more concentrated decision distributions, stronger consensus, and higher cross-model robustness of correctness. These findings suggest that evaluating agentic systems through accuracy or agreement alone may not always be sufficient, and that complementary analyses of stability, cross-model robustness, and potential clinical impact are needed to characterize reliability under model variability.

### [113] [Stem: Rethinking Causal Information Flow in Sparse Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06274)
*Lin Niu,Xin Luo,Linchuan Xie,Yifu Sun,Guanghua Yu,Jianchen Zhu,S Kevin Zhou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出Stem，一种即插即用的稀疏注意力模块，通过Token位置衰减策略和输出感知度量，在降低计算复杂度和预填充延迟的同时保持高精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自注意力的二次计算复杂度是扩展大型语言模型处理长上下文的主要瓶颈，尤其在预填充阶段。现有的稀疏方法在各层中采用统一的top-k选择，忽略了因果架构中token信息的累积依赖性。

Method: 提出Stem模块，包含两个核心组件：(1) Token位置衰减策略，在每层应用位置依赖的top-k选择，保留初始token以维持递归依赖；(2) 输出感知度量，基于近似输出幅值优先选择高影响力token。

Result: 广泛评估表明，Stem在减少计算量和预填充延迟的同时，实现了更优的准确率。

Conclusion: Stem通过将稀疏策略与信息流对齐，有效解决了因果注意力中的信息累积问题，为长上下文LLM提供了高效的解决方案。

Abstract: The quadratic computational complexity of self-attention remains a fundamental bottleneck for scaling Large Language Models (LLMs) to long contexts, particularly during the pre-filling phase. In this paper, we rethink the causal attention mechanism from the perspective of information flow. Due to causal constraints, tokens at initial positions participate in the aggregation of every subsequent token. However, existing sparse methods typically apply a uniform top-k selection across all token positions within a layer, ignoring the cumulative dependency of token information inherent in causal architectures. To address this, we propose Stem, a novel, plug-and-play sparsity module aligned with information flow. First, Stem employs the Token Position-Decay strategy, applying position-dependent top-k within each layer to retain initial tokens for recursive dependencies. Second, to preserve information-rich tokens, Stem utilizes the Output-Aware Metric. It prioritizes high-impact tokens based on approximate output magnitude. Extensive evaluations demonstrate that Stem achieves superior accuracy with reduced computation and pre-filling latency.

### [114] [From Entropy to Calibrated Uncertainty: Training Language Models to Reason About Uncertainty](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06317)
*Azza Jenane,Nassim Walha,Lukas Kuhn,Florian Buettner*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种三阶段流程，通过后训练使大型语言模型能够高效推断出经过校准的不确定性估计，在推理时兼具可解释性与计算效率，并展现出良好的泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高风险领域中，大型语言模型（LLM）能够表达可解释且校准的不确定性至关重要。然而，现有的后处理不确定性估计方法通常基于采样，计算成本高昂或缺乏校准性。

Method: 提出三阶段流程：首先在训练数据上计算细粒度的基于熵的不确定性分数，捕捉嵌入空间中模型输出的分布变异性；其次通过Platt缩放对这些分数进行校准，生成可靠且人类可解释的不确定性信号；最后利用强化学习对目标LLM进行后训练，通过可验证的奖励函数使其策略与校准后的信号对齐。

Result: 实验表明，经过该流程训练的模型在校准性上优于基线方法，并能泛化到未见过的任务且无需额外处理，表明模型学习到了鲁棒的不确定性推理行为。

Conclusion: 与后处理不确定性估计方法不同，该方法在测试时提供可解释且计算高效的不确定性估计，使LLM具备了鲁棒的不确定性推理能力。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) that can express interpretable and calibrated uncertainty are crucial in high-stakes domains. While methods to compute uncertainty post-hoc exist, they are often sampling-based and therefore computationally expensive or lack calibration. We propose a three-stage pipeline to post-train LLMs to efficiently infer calibrated uncertainty estimates for their responses. First, we compute fine-grained entropy-based uncertainty scores on the training data, capturing the distributional variability of model outputs in embedding space. Second, these scores are calibrated via Platt scaling, producing reliable and human-interpretable uncertainty signals. Finally, the target LLM is post-trained via reinforcement learning to align its policy with these calibrated signals through a verifiable reward function. Unlike post-hoc uncertainty estimation methods, our approach provides interpretable and computationally efficient uncertainty estimates at test time. Experiments show that models trained with our pipeline achieve better calibration than baselines and generalize to unseen tasks without further processing, suggesting that they learn a robust uncertainty reasoning behavior.

</details>


### [115] [Topological descriptors of foot clearance gait dynamics improve differential diagnosis of Parkinsonism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06212)

Method: 采用拓扑数据分析(TDA)作为帕金森综合征分类的补充工具，使用持续同调生成Betti曲线、持续景观和轮廓，将这些拓扑特征输入随机森林分类器。数据集包含15名对照组、15名特发性帕金森病(IPD)和14名血管性帕金森综合征(VaP)，采用留一法交叉验证(LOOCV)评估模型。

Conclusion: 研究结果支持将TDA与机器学习相结合以改进临床步态分析，辅助帕金森综合征的鉴别诊断，为临床决策提供有价值的工具。

Abstract: Differential diagnosis among parkinsonian syndromes remains a clinical challenge due to overlapping motor symptoms and subtle gait abnormalities. Accurate differentiation is crucial for treatment planning and prognosis. While gait analysis is a well established approach for assessing motor impairments, conventional methods often overlook hidden nonlinear and structural features embedded in foot clearance patterns. We evaluated Topological Data Analysis (TDA) as a complementary tool for Parkinsonism classification using foot clearance time series. Persistent homology produced Betti curves, persistence landscapes, and silhouettes, which were used as features for a Random Forest classifier. The dataset comprised 15 controls (CO), 15 idiopathic Parkinson's disease (IPD), and 14 vascular Parkinsonism (VaP). Models were assessed with leave-one-out cross-validation (LOOCV). Betti-curve descriptors consistently yielded the strongest results. For IPD vs VaP, foot clearance variables minimum toe clearance, maximum toe late swing, and maximum heel clearance achieved 83% accuracy and AUC=0.89 under LOOCV in the medicated (On) state. Performance improved in the On state and further when both Off and On states were considered, indicating sensitivity of the topological features to levodopa related gait changes. These findings support integrating TDA with machine learning to improve clinical gait analysis and aid differential diagnosis across parkinsonian disorders.

Abstract: Accurate fault detection in high-dimensional industrial environments remains a major challenge due to the inherent complexity, noise, and redundancy in sensor data. The learned representations are then fed into a downstream classifier to perform binary fault prediction. Experimental results on a high-dimensional dataset demonstrate that CLAIRE significantly outperforms conventional classifiers trained directly on raw features. Moreover, the framework incorporates a post hoc phase, using a game-theory-based interpretability technique, to analyze the latent space and identify the most informative input features contributing to fault predictions. The proposed framework highlights the potential of integrating explainable AI with feature-aware regularization for robust fault detection. ### [118] [NOBLE: Accelerating Transformers with Nonlinear Low-Rank Branches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06492)
*Ethan Smith*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: NOBLE是一种通过在Transformer线性层中添加非线性低秩分支来加速预训练的架构增强方法，能够在仅增加4%参数和7%时间开销的情况下，实现最高1.47倍的收敛加速和1.22倍的实际训练时间节省。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的参数高效微调方法（如LoRA）主要针对预训练模型的微调场景，而本文旨在探索低秩结构是否可以在从头预训练阶段发挥作用，通过将其作为架构的永久组成部分来提升训练效率。

Method: NOBLE在Transformer的线性层中添加非线性低秩分支，计算形式为σ(xW_down)W_up，其中σ为可学习的非线性激活函数。经过对比多种激活函数，作者提出CosNet（一种包含可学习频率和相位的两层余弦非线性函数，在瓶颈空间中夹带线性投影）作为最优选择。该分支是架构的永久部分，而非适配器。

Result: 在LLM（250M和1.5B参数）、BERT、VQGAN和ViT上的实验表明，NOBLE仅增加4%的参数量和7%的单步时间开销，即可实现高达1.47倍的收敛加速（减少32%训练步数）和1.22倍的实际训练时间节省。研究发现Mixup/CutMix等随机数据增强会干扰NOBLE的效果，可能因为NOBLE更擅长拟合目标函数的尖锐特征，而正则化技术鼓励更平滑的拟合。

Conclusion: NOBLE证明非线性低秩分支作为架构增强可以有效加速从头预训练过程，在多种模型和任务上表现出一致的训练效率提升。该方法与某些随机数据增强技术存在不兼容性，这揭示了低秩非线性分支可能与正则化策略在拟合目标函数的特性上存在差异。

Abstract: We introduce NOBLE (Nonlinear lOw-rank Branch for Linear Enhancement), an architectural augmentation that adds nonlinear low-rank branches to transformer linear layers. Unlike LoRA and other parameter-efficient fine-tuning (PEFT) methods, NOBLE is designed for pretraining from scratch. The branch is a permanent part of the architecture as opposed to an adapter for finetuning on top of frozen weights. The branch computes σ(xWdown)Wup where σ is a learnable nonlinearity. We evaluate several activation functions and find that CosNet, a two-layer cosine nonlinearity with learnable frequency and phase with a linear projection in between them in the bottleneck space, performs best. NOBLE achieves substantial improvements with minimal overhead: up to 1.47x step speedup to reach baseline eval loss (up to 32% fewer training steps), with as low as 4% additional parameters and 7% step time overhead, resulting in up to 1.22x net wallclock speedup. Experiments on LLMs (250M and 1.5B parameters), BERT, VQGAN, and ViT consistently show improved training efficiency. We identify one caveat: Mixup/CutMix augmentation interferes with NOBLE's benefits in Imagenet classification along with other stochastic augmentations, but when disabled, ViT also improves. This discrepancy is possibly explained by regularization techniques that encourage smoother fits to the target function while NOBLE may specialize more in sharper aspects of the target function.

</details>


### [119] [DC-Merge: Improving Model Merging with Directional Consistency](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06242)
*Han-Chen Zhang,Zi-Hao Zhou,Mao-Lin Luo,Shimin Di,Min-Ling Zhang,Tong Wei*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了DC-Merge方法，通过平滑奇异值平衡能量分布并将任务向量投影到共享正交子空间来解决模型合并中的方向不一致问题，在视觉和视觉语言基准测试中实现了最先进的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 模型合并旨在将多个任务适配模型整合为统一模型，但关键挑战在于保持合并后的多任务向量与单个任务向量之间奇异空间的方向一致性。现有方法面临两个问题：一是任务向量内能量分布不平衡，少量奇异值主导总能量导致合并时忽略语义重要但较弱的成分；二是参数空间中任务向量的几何不一致性导致直接合并扭曲其潜在的方向几何结构。

Method: DC-Merge包含三个关键步骤：首先通过平滑奇异值来平衡每个任务向量的能量分布，确保所有知识成分得到充分表示；然后将这些能量平衡的向量投影到共享正交子空间，以最小的重构误差对齐其方向几何结构；最后在共享正交子空间中聚合对齐后的向量并投影回原始参数空间。

Result: 在视觉和视觉语言基准测试上进行了大量实验，结果表明DC-Merge在全量微调和LoRA设置下均持续实现最先进的性能表现。

Conclusion: DC-Merge通过解决能量分布不平衡和几何不一致性问题，成功实现了方向一致的模型合并，为多任务模型整合提供了有效解决方案，代码已开源。

Abstract: Model merging aims to integrate multiple task-adapted models into a unified model that preserves the knowledge of each task. In this paper, we identify that the key to this knowledge retention lies in maintaining the directional consistency of singular spaces between merged multi-task vector and individual task vectors. However, this consistency is frequently compromised by two issues: i) an imbalanced energy distribution within task vectors, where a small fraction of singular values dominate the total energy, leading to the neglect of semantically important but weaker components upon merging, and ii) the geometric inconsistency of task vectors in parameter space, which causes direct merging to distort their underlying directional geometry. To address these challenges, we propose DC-Merge, a method for directional-consistent model merging. It first balances the energy distribution of each task vector by smoothing its singular values, ensuring all knowledge components are adequately represented. These energy-balanced vectors are then projected onto a shared orthogonal subspace to align their directional geometries with minimal reconstruction error. Finally, the aligned vectors are aggregated in the shared orthogonal subspace and projected back to the original parameter space. Extensive experiments on vision and vision-language benchmarks show that DC-Merge consistently achieves state-of-the-art performance in both full fine-tuning and LoRA settings. The implementation code is available at https://github.com/Tobeginwith/DC-Merge.

</details>


### [120] [COLD-Steer: Steering Large Language Models via In-Context One-step Learning Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06495)
*Kartik Sharma,Rakshit S. Trivedi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了COLD-Steer框架，一种无需训练的LLM激活引导方法，通过近似梯度下降在上下文示例上的表示变化来实现推理时控制，在减少50倍样本量的同时达到高达95%的引导效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的激活引导方法存在基本权衡：样本高效的方法对标记示例中引导信号的捕获效果欠佳，而能够更好提取信号的方法需要数百到数千个示例。需要一种既能高效利用少量示例，又能充分提取引导信号的方法。

Method: 提出COLD-Steer框架，通过近似在上下文示例上进行梯度下降所产生的表示变化来引导LLM激活，无需实际参数更新。包含两种互补方法：(i)单元核近似方法，直接使用关于激活的梯度更新激活，并在示例间进行归一化；(ii)有限差分近似方法，无论示例数量多少仅需两次前向传递。

Result: 在各种引导任务和基准测试中，COLD-Steer在比最佳基线减少50倍样本量的情况下，实现了高达95%的引导效果。在多元化对齐任务上也验证了该方法能够用较少演示数据适应多样化观点。

Conclusion: COLD-Steer框架通过有原则地近似学习动态而非专门训练程序，为自适应、上下文感知的模型控制开辟了新可能，能够灵活地处理基于损失的人类偏好差异。

Abstract: Activation steering methods enable inference-time control of large language model (LLM) behavior without retraining, but current approaches face a fundamental trade-off: sample-efficient methods suboptimally capture steering signals from labeled examples, while methods that better extract these signals require hundreds to thousands of examples. We introduce COLD-Steer, a training-free framework that steers LLM activations by approximating the representational changes that would result from gradient descent on in-context examples. Our key insight is that the effect of fine-tuning on a small set of examples can be efficiently approximated at inference time without actual parameter updates. We formalize this through two complementary approaches: (i) a unit kernel approximation method that updates the activations directly using gradients with respect to them, normalized across examples, and (ii) a finite-difference approximation requiring only two forward passes regardless of example count. Experiments across a variety of steering tasks and benchmarks demonstrate that COLD-Steer achieves upto 95% steering effectiveness while using 50 times fewer samples compared to the best baseline. COLD-Steer facilitates accommodating diverse perspectives without extensive demonstration data, which we validate through our experiments on pluralistic alignment tasks. Our framework opens new possibilities for adaptive, context-aware model control that can flexibly address varying loss-driven human preferences through principled approximation of learning dynamics rather than specialized training procedures.

### [121] [Gradient Flow Polarizes Softmax Outputs towards Low-Entropy Solutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06248)
*Aditya Varre,Mark Rofin,Nicolas Flammarion*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文分析了值-softmax模型的梯度流动力学，揭示了softmax结构固有的低熵输出偏好，为注意力汇聚和大规模激活等现象提供了理论解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解softmax模型非凸训练动力学对解释Transformer的经验成功至关重要，矩阵乘softmax向量参数化是自注意力的核心构建块，因此研究该结构的梯度流动力学能直接洞察Transformer的训练动态。

Method: 分析值-softmax模型L(Vσ(a))的梯度流动力学，其中V和a分别是可学习的值矩阵和注意力向量，研究在不同目标函数（包括逻辑损失和平方损失）下的优化轨迹。

Result: 证明了该结构上的梯度流固有地将优化推向低熵输出的解；揭示了这种极化效应在各种目标函数下的普适性；为注意力汇聚和大规模激活等经验现象提供了形式化机制。

Conclusion: softmax结构本身具有诱导低熵输出的内在倾向，这一理论发现解释了Transformer训练中观察到的多种经验现象，为理解深度注意力模型的训练动力学提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Understanding the intricate non-convex training dynamics of softmax-based models is crucial for explaining the empirical success of transformers. In this article, we analyze the gradient flow dynamics of the value-softmax model, defined as ${L}(\mathbf{V} σ(\mathbf{a}))$, where $\mathbf{V}$ and $\mathbf{a}$ are a learnable value matrix and attention vector, respectively. As the matrix times softmax vector parameterization constitutes the core building block of self-attention, our analysis provides direct insight into transformer's training dynamics. We reveal that gradient flow on this structure inherently drives the optimization toward solutions characterized by low-entropy outputs. We demonstrate the universality of this polarizing effect across various objectives, including logistic and square loss. Furthermore, we discuss the practical implications of these theoretical results, offering a formal mechanism for empirical phenomena such as attention sinks and massive activations.

Method: 引入合成监控环境（SMEs）——一个无限的连续控制任务套件。该框架提供完全可配置的任务特性、已知的最优策略、严格的几何状态空间边界，支持精确计算瞬时遗憾，并允许系统性的分布内（WD）和分布外（OOD）评估。

Abstract: Reinforcement Learning (RL) lacks benchmarks that enable precise, white-box diagnostics of agent behavior. Current environments often entangle complexity factors and lack ground-truth optimality metrics, making it difficult to isolate why algorithms fail. We introduce Synthetic Monitoring Environments (SMEs), an infinite suite of continuous control tasks. SMEs provide fully configurable task characteristics and known optimal policies. As such, SMEs allow for the exact calculation of instantaneous regret. Their rigorous geometric state space bounds allow for systematic within-distribution (WD) and out-of-distribution (OOD) evaluation. We demonstrate the framework's benefit through multidimensional ablations of PPO, TD3, and SAC, revealing how specific environmental properties - such as action or state space size, reward sparsity and complexity of the optimal policy - impact WD and OOD performance. We thereby show that SMEs offer a standardized, transparent testbed for transitioning RL evaluation from empirical benchmarking toward rigorous scientific analysis.

### [124] [Frequency-Separable Hamiltonian Neural Network for Multi-Timescale Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06354)
*Yaojun Li,Yulong Yang,Christine Allen-Blanchette*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于哈密顿函数可分解为显式快慢模式的观察，提出频率可分离哈密顿神经网络（FS-HNN）。该方法使用多个神经网络参数化系统哈密顿函数，每个网络由哈密顿动力学控制，并在不同的时间尺度上采样训练。进一步将该框架扩展至偏微分方程，通过学习状态和边界条件的辛算子进行建模。

Abstract: While Hamiltonian mechanics provides a powerful inductive bias for neural networks modeling dynamical systems, Hamiltonian Neural Networks and their variants often fail to capture complex temporal dynamics spanning multiple timescales. This limitation is commonly linked to the spectral bias of deep neural networks, which favors learning low-frequency, slow-varying dynamics. Prior approaches have sought to address this issue through symplectic integration schemes that enforce energy conservation or by incorporating geometric constraints to impose structure on the configuration-space. However, such methods either remain limited in their ability to fully capture multiscale dynamics or require substantial domain specific assumptions. In this work, we exploit the observation that Hamiltonian functions admit decompositions into explicit fast and slow modes and can be reconstructed from these components. We introduce the Frequency-Separable Hamiltonian Neural Network (FS-HNN), which parameterizes the system Hamiltonian using multiple networks, each governed by Hamiltonian dynamics and trained on data sampled at distinct timescales. We further extend this framework to partial differential equations by learning a state- and boundary-conditioned symplectic operators. Empirically, we show that FS-HNN improves long-horizon extrapolation performance on challenging dynamical systems and generalizes across a broad range of ODE and PDE problems.

However, state-of-the-art machine learning methods require vast amounts of labelled user data, making them unsuitable for models that reside client-side and only have access to a single user's data. State-of-the-art methods are also computationally expensive, which degrades the user experience on compute-limited hardware and also reduces battery life. A recent alternative approach has proven remarkably successful in classification tasks across a wide variety of data -- using a compression-based distance measure (called normalised compression distance) to measure the distance between generic objects in classical distance-based machine learning methods. In this work, we demonstrate that the normalised compression distance is actually not a metric; develop it for the wider context of kernel methods to allow modelling of complex data; and present techniques to improve the training time of models that use this distance measure. ### [126] [Adaptive Lipschitz-Free Conditional Gradient Methods for Stochastic Composite Nonconvex Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06369)
*Ganzhao Yuan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了ALFCG，首个针对随机复合非凸优化问题的自适应无投影框架，无需全局平滑常数或线搜索，在噪声趋近于零时可达到最优的$\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(ε^{-2})$收敛率。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的条件梯度方法存在局限性：使用开环递减步长、保守的Lipschitz常数或高昂的回溯策略，无法有效适应未知的几何结构。因此需要一种既能保持Frank-Wolfe方法简洁性，又能自适应估计局部平滑度的无投影优化框架。

Method: 提出ALFCG框架，通过维护历史迭代差值的自归一化累加器来估计局部平滑度，并在每步最小化二次代理模型。设计了三种变体：(1)ALFCG-FS针对有限和问题使用SPIDER估计器；(2)ALFCG-MVR1和ALFCG-MVR2处理随机期望问题，分别采用单批次和双批次更新的动量方差缩减策略，分别在平均平滑度和个体平滑度假设下运行。

Result: ALFCG-FS达到$\mathcal{O}(N+\sqrt{N}ε^{-2})$迭代复杂度；ALFCG-MVR1和ALFCG-MVR2分别达到$\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(σ^2ε^{-4}+ε^{-2})$和$\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(σε^{-3}+ε^{-2})$。与典型的$\mathcal{O}(ε^{-4})$或$\mathcal{O}(ε^{-3})$速率相比，当噪声水平σ→0时，算法收敛率可降为最优的$\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(ε^{-2})$。在核范数球和$\ell_p$球上的多分类实验中，ALFCG优于现有最先进的条件梯度基线方法。

Conclusion: ALFCG成功实现了无需全局平滑常数或线搜索的自适应无投影优化，在理论复杂度和实际性能上均优于现有方法，为随机复合非凸优化问题提供了更高效的解决方案。

Abstract: We propose ALFCG (Adaptive Lipschitz-Free Conditional Gradient), the first \textit{adaptive} projection-free framework for stochastic composite nonconvex minimization that \textit{requires neither global smoothness constants nor line search}. Unlike prior conditional gradient methods that use openloop diminishing stepsizes, conservative Lipschitz constants, or costly backtracking, ALFCG maintains a self-normalized accumulator of historical iterate differences to estimate local smoothness and minimize a quadratic surrogate model at each step. This retains the simplicity of Frank-Wolfe while adapting to unknown geometry. We study three variants. ALFCG-FS addresses finite-sum problems with a SPIDER estimator. ALFCG-MVR1 and ALFCG-MVR2 handle stochastic expectation problems by using momentum-based variance reduction with single-batch and two-batch updates, and operate under average and individual smoothness, respectively. To reach an $ε$-stationary point, ALFCG-FS attains $\mathcal{O}(N+\sqrt{N}ε^{-2})$ iteration complexity, while ALFCG-MVR1 and ALFCG-MVR2 achieve $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(σ^2ε^{-4}+ε^{-2})$ and $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(σε^{-3}+ε^{-2})$, where $N$ is the number of components and $σ$ is the noise level. In contrast to typical $\mathcal{O}(ε^{-4})$ or $\mathcal{O}(ε^{-3})$ rates, our bounds reduce to the optimal rate up to logarithmic factors $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(ε^{-2})$ as the noise level $σ\to 0$. Extensive experiments on multiclass classification over nuclear norm balls and $\ell_p$ balls show that ALFCG generally outperforms state-of-the-art conditional gradient baselines.

</details>


### [127] [Adapter-Augmented Bandits for Online Multi-Constrained Multi-Modal Inference Scheduling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06403)
*Xianzhi Zhang,Yue Xu,Yinlin Zhu,Di Wu,Yipeng Zhou,Miao Hu,Guocong Quan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出M-CMAB框架，通过多适配器增强的多臂老虎机方法解决多模态大语言模型在线推理调度问题，在异构后端和预算约束下实现比现有方法高14.18%的奖励。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多模态大语言模型的在线推理调度面临双重挑战：（1）请求在模态组成和潜在推理难度上差异显著，难以提取既保持语义忠实又适用于调度的任务表示；（2）执行后端因系统抖动和网络变化产生差异化的时变成本，需在不可逆的多维预算约束下做出低开销的在线决策。

Method: 提出M-CMAB框架，包含三个核心组件：（i）CLS注意力冻结骨干预测器，提取紧凑任务表示并仅更新轻量级适配器以进行动作特定估计；（ii）原始-对偶约束器，通过在线拉格朗日乘子在每轮目标中强制执行长时域约束；（iii）两阶段调度器，在不可逆预算下平衡探索与利用。

Result: 在包含异构后端的复合多模态基准测试中，M-CMAB在各预算机制下持续优于最先进基线，奖励提升高达14.18%，并紧密追踪oracle辅助的上界。论文还建立了多维背包约束下的遗憾保证。

Conclusion: M-CMAB成功解决了多模态大语言模型推理调度中任务表示和在线决策的核心挑战，通过理论保证和实验验证证明了其在异构预算约束场景下的有效性，为实际部署提供了可行的解决方案。

Abstract: Multi-modal large language model (MLLM) inference scheduling enables strong response quality under practical and heterogeneous budgets, beyond what a homogeneous single-backend setting can offer. Yet online MLLM task scheduling is nontrivial, as requests vary sharply in modality composition and latent reasoning difficulty, while execution backends incur distinct, time-varying costs due to system jitter and network variation. These coupled uncertainties pose two core challenges: deriving semantically faithful yet scheduling-relevant multi-modal task representations, and making low-overhead online decisions over irreversible multi-dimensional budgets. Accordingly, we propose \emph{M-CMAB} (\underline{M}ulti-modal \underline{M}ulti-constraint \underline{C}ontextual \underline{M}ulti-\underline{A}rmed \underline{B}andit), a multi-adapter-enhanced MLLM inference scheduling framework with three components: (i) a CLS-attentive, frozen-backbone \emph{Predictor} that extracts compact task representations and updates only lightweight adapters for action-specific estimation; (ii) a primal-dual \emph{Constrainer} that maintains online Lagrange multipliers to enforce long-horizon constraints via per-round objectives; and (iii) a two-phase \emph{Scheduler} that balances exploration and exploitation under irreversible budgets. We establish a regret guarantee under multi-dimensional knapsack constraints. On a composite multimodal benchmark with heterogeneous backends, \emph{M-CMAB} consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines across budget regimes, achieving up to 14.18% higher reward and closely tracking an oracle-aided upper bound. Codes are available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/M2CMAB/.

</details>


### [128] [Toward Generative Quantum Utility via Correlation-Complexity Map](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06440)
*Chen-Yu Liu,Leonardo Placidi,Eric Brunner,Enrico Rinaldi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种相关性-复杂度映射方法，用于诊断现实数据分布是否适合IQP型量子生成模型。该方法通过量子相关性指标（QCLI）和经典相关性复杂度指标（CCI）量化数据特征，并在湍流数据上验证了IQP模型的优越性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 确定现实世界数据分布何时与IQP型量子生成模型结构对齐是一个开放性问题。现有的量子生成模型应用缺乏有效的诊断工具来判断特定数据是否适合采用量子方法，这限制了量子生成模型的实用价值。因此需要开发实用的诊断指标来识别量子优势领域。

Method: 提出相关性-复杂度映射框架，包含两个互补指标：（1）量子相关性指标（QCLI）：基于数据集的相关性阶次（Walsh-Hadamard/傅里叶）功率谱，按交互阶次聚合并通过Jensen-Shannon散度与i.i.d.二项分布参考进行量化；（2）经典相关性复杂度指标（CCI）：定义为总相关性中未被最优Chow-Liu树近似捕获的比例，经总相关性归一化。理论证明较高QCLI意味着固定架构IQP族在MMD目标下具有更低的不可约近似误差下限。基于映射定位，采用可逆浮点-比特串表示和潜参数自适应方案，在时间序列上复用紧凑IQP电路。

Result: 将经典湍流数据识别为既IQP兼容又具有经典复杂性（高QCLI/高CCI）。在对比评估中，IQP方法与受限玻尔兹曼机（RBM）和深度卷积生成对抗网络（DCGAN）等经典模型相比，实现了竞争性的分布对齐，同时使用了显著更少的训练快照和更小的潜变量块，验证了QCLI/CCI作为实用指标的有效性。

Conclusion: QCLI/CCI指标为定位IQP对齐领域提供了实用的诊断工具，有助于推进量子生成模型的实用性。相关性-复杂度映射能够有效识别适合量子生成模型的数据分布，为量子生成优势的实际应用提供了指导框架。

Abstract: We propose a Correlation-Complexity Map as a practical diagnostic tool for determining when real-world data distributions are structurally aligned with IQP-type quantum generative models. Characterized by two complementary indicators: (i) a Quantum Correlation-Likeness Indicator (QCLI), computed from the dataset's correlation-order (Walsh-Hadamard/Fourier) power spectrum aggregated by interaction order and quantified via Jensen-Shannon divergence from an i.i.d. binomial reference; and (ii) a Classical Correlation-Complexity Indicator (CCI), defined as the fraction of total correlation not captured by the optimal Chow-Liu tree approximation, normalized by total correlation. We provide theoretical support by relating QCLI to a support-mismatch mechanism, for fixed-architecture IQP families trained with an MMD objective, higher QCLI implies a smaller irreducible approximation floor. Using the map, we identify the classical turbulence data as both IQP-compatible and classically complex (high QCLI/high CCI). Guided by this placement, we use an invertible float-to-bitstring representation and a latent-parameter adaptation scheme that reuses a compact IQP circuit over a temporal sequence by learning and interpolating a low-dimensional latent trajectory. In comparative evaluations against classical models such as Restricted Boltzmann Machine (RBM) and Deep Convolutional Generative Adversarial Networks (DCGAN), the IQP approach achieves competitive distributional alignment while using substantially fewer training snapshots and a small latent block, supporting the use of QCLI/CCI as practical indicators for locating IQP-aligned domains and advancing generative quantum utility.

</details>


### [129] [When One Modality Rules Them All: Backdoor Modality Collapse in Multimodal Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06508)
*Qitong Wang,Haoran Dai,Haotian Zhang,Christopher Rasmussen,Binghui Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文挑战了多模态扩散模型中“攻击多模态可产生协同增强效果”的直觉假设，揭示了后门攻击中存在的“模态坍缩”现象：攻击往往退化为仅依赖部分模态，而跨模态交互微乎其微甚至为负，表明高攻击成功率掩盖了对特定模态的依赖这一关键盲点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散模型在视觉生成领域广泛应用，其后门安全漏洞研究至关重要。在多模态扩散模型中，人们普遍直觉认为同时攻击多个模态（如文本和图像）会产生互补效应并增强后门效果。然而，这一假设缺乏严格验证，促使作者探究多模态后门攻击的真实机制。

Method: 提出“后门模态坍缩”（Backdoor Modality Collapse）概念，并设计两个新的量化指标：触发器模态归因（TMA）用于度量后门对不同模态的依赖程度，跨触发器交互（CTI）用于量化模态间的相互作用。通过在多种多模态条件扩散模型训练配置下进行广泛实验，系统分析后门行为模式。

Result: 实验一致观察到后门行为中存在“赢者通吃”动态：（1）攻击经常坍缩为子模态主导，即后门机制主要依赖部分模态而使其他模态冗余；（2）跨模态交互可忽略不计甚至为负值。这与多模态协同脆弱性的直觉相矛盾，表明高攻击成功率往往掩盖了对特定模态子集的根本性依赖。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了当前安全评估中的关键盲点，证明了多模态后门攻击并非天然具有协同优势，而是倾向于模态坍缩。这一发现为后门机制分析提供了新视角，并为未来防御策略的开发奠定了原则性基础，促使研究者在评估多模态模型安全性时需更深入地审视模态依赖关系。

Abstract: While diffusion models have revolutionized visual content generation, their rapid adoption has underscored the critical need to investigate vulnerabilities, e.g., to backdoor attacks. In multimodal diffusion models, it is natural to expect that attacking multiple modalities simultaneously (e.g., text and image) would yield complementary effects and strengthen the overall backdoor. In this paper, we challenge this assumption by investigating the phenomenon of Backdoor Modality Collapse, a scenario where the backdoor mechanism degenerates to rely predominantly on a subset of modalities, rendering others redundant. To rigorously quantify this behavior, we introduce two novel metrics: Trigger Modality Attribution (TMA) and Cross-Trigger Interaction (CTI). Through extensive experiments across diverse training configurations in multimodal conditional diffusion, we consistently observe a ``winner-takes-all'' dynamic in backdoor behavior. Our results reveal that (1) attacks often collapse into subset-modality dominance, and (2) cross-modal interaction is negligible or even negative, contradicting the intuition of synergistic vulnerability. These findings highlight a critical blind spot in current assessments, suggesting that high attack success rates often mask a fundamental reliance on a subset of modalities. This establishes a principled foundation for mechanistic analysis and future defense development.

</details>

Furthermore, we provide multiple real-world case studies that show the efficacy of our approach in identifying important patterns and explanations that help stakeholders better understand the forecasts. ### [131] [Causal Interpretation of Neural Network Computations with Contribution Decomposition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06557)
*Joshua Brendan Melander,Zaki Alaoui,Shenghua Liu,Surya Ganguli,Stephen A. Baccus*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出CODEC方法，利用稀疏自编码器将网络行为分解为隐藏神经元贡献的稀疏模式，揭示了仅靠激活分析无法确定的因果过程，并在图像分类网络和视网膜神经活动模型中验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法主要通过分析隐藏层激活模式与人类可解释概念的相关性来理解神经网络，但这种方法无法直接揭示隐藏神经元如何驱动网络输出的因果过程。因此需要一种直接分析隐藏神经元贡献的方法来理解神经网络的内部机制。

Method: 提出CODEC（贡献分解）方法，使用稀疏自编码器将网络行为分解为隐藏神经元贡献的稀疏模式（sparse motifs），从而揭示神经元对输出的贡献方式，而非仅仅分析激活模式。

Result: 在图像分类网络中发现贡献在层级间稀疏性和维度增加，且正负效应逐渐去相关；分解后的稀疏模式支持对网络输出的因果操控和可视化；在视网膜神经活动模型中揭示了模型中间神经元的组合作用和动态感受野的来源。

Conclusion: CODEC为理解非线性计算如何在层级结构中演化提供了丰富且可解释的框架，确立了贡献模式作为分析人工神经网络机制洞察的信息单元。

Abstract: Understanding how neural networks transform inputs into outputs is crucial for interpreting and manipulating their behavior. Most existing approaches analyze internal representations by identifying hidden-layer activation patterns correlated with human-interpretable concepts. Here we take a direct approach to examine how hidden neurons act to drive network outputs. We introduce CODEC (Contribution Decomposition), a method that uses sparse autoencoders to decompose network behavior into sparse motifs of hidden-neuron contributions, revealing causal processes that cannot be determined by analyzing activations alone. Applying CODEC to benchmark image-classification networks, we find that contributions grow in sparsity and dimensionality across layers and, unexpectedly, that they progressively decorrelate positive and negative effects on network outputs. We further show that decomposing contributions into sparse modes enables greater control and interpretation of intermediate layers, supporting both causal manipulations of network output and human-interpretable visualizations of distinct image components that combine to drive that output. Finally, by analyzing state-of-the-art models of neural activity in the vertebrate retina, we demonstrate that CODEC uncovers combinatorial actions of model interneurons and identifies the sources of dynamic receptive fields. Overall, CODEC provides a rich and interpretable framework for understanding how nonlinear computations evolve across hierarchical layers, establishing contribution modes as an informative unit of analysis for mechanistic insights into artificial neural networks.

### [132] [A recipe for scalable attention-based MLIPs: unlocking long-range accuracy with all-to-all node attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06567)
*Eric Qu,Brandon M. Wood,Aditi S. Krishnapriyan,Zachary W. Ulissi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了AllScAIP，一种基于全注意力机制、能量守恒的机器学习原子间势模型，可扩展至亿级训练样本。通过数据驱动的全节点注意力组件解决长程相互作用问题，在分子系统及多项物理基准测试中达到SOTA精度，并支持稳定的长时间分子动力学模拟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有机器学习原子间势（MLIPs）在大尺度系统（如生物分子和电解质）中难以准确捕捉长程相互作用，当前方法依赖显式物理项或组件。需要一种能随数据和模型规模扩展、无需强物理归纳偏置的方案。

Method: 提出AllScAIP模型，采用全节点注意力组件以数据驱动方式捕捉长程相互作用，设计简单、注意力机制驱动且保证能量守恒，可扩展至约1亿训练样本。通过大规模消融实验分析归纳偏置与注意力机制在不同数据/模型规模下的作用。

Result: 在分子系统上达到SOTA能量/力预测精度；在OMol25、OMat24、OC20等基准测试中表现优异或具竞争力；支持稳定的长时分子动力学模拟，能准确复现实验可观测值（如密度和汽化热）。消融实验发现：在低数据/小模型 regime 下归纳偏置提升样本效率，但随着数据和模型规模增大，其优势减弱甚至逆转，而全注意力机制对捕捉长程相互作用始终关键。

Conclusion: 随着数据和模型规模增长，显式物理归纳偏置的收益递减，而数据驱动的全注意力机制成为解决长程相互作用的关键。AllScAIP展示了纯注意力模型在大规模MLIP任务中的潜力，为构建通用、可扩展的原子间势模型提供了新方向。

Abstract: Machine-learning interatomic potentials (MLIPs) have advanced rapidly, with many top models relying on strong physics-based inductive biases. However, as models scale to larger systems like biomolecules and electrolytes, they struggle to accurately capture long-range (LR) interactions, leading current approaches to rely on explicit physics-based terms or components. In this work, we propose AllScAIP, a straightforward, attention-based, and energy-conserving MLIP model that scales to O(100 million) training samples. It addresses the long-range challenge using an all-to-all node attention component that is data-driven. Extensive ablations reveal that in low-data/small-model regimes, inductive biases improve sample efficiency. However, as data and model size scale, these benefits diminish or even reverse, while all-to-all attention remains critical for capturing LR interactions. Our model achieves state-of-the-art energy/force accuracy on molecular systems, as well as a number of physics-based evaluations (OMol25), while being competitive on materials (OMat24) and catalysts (OC20). Furthermore, it enables stable, long-timescale MD simulations that accurately recover experimental observables, including density and heat of vaporization predictions.

</details>

### [133] [CrossCheck: Input Validation for WAN Control Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05792)
*Alexander Krentsel,Rishabh Iyer,Isaac Keslassy,Bharath Modhipalli,Sylvia Ratnasamy,Anees Shaikh,Rob Shakir*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文提出了CrossCheck系统，用于验证广域网（WAN）中SDN控制器的输入。通过检测错误输入，CrossCheck能够在网络中断发生前预警运营商。在大型WAN运营商部署中，该系统准确检测到唯一一次无效输入事件，保持0%误报率，并能检测小至5%的需求扰动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 作者在大型WAN运营商处分析发现，无效输入是导致重大网络中断的主要原因，而这些无效输入通常源于SDN控制基础设施中的漏洞。为了在网络中断发生前预防此类问题，作者提出了CrossCheck系统来验证SDN控制器的输入。

Method: CrossCheck是一个SDN控制器输入验证系统，部署为影子验证系统（shadow validation system）。它通过验证输入数据的正确性来检测潜在问题，能够处理嘈杂、缺失或错误的遥测数据。作者采用了四周的生产WAN部署和大规模仿真测试相结合的方法。

Result: 在四周的生产WAN部署中，CrossCheck准确检测到唯一一次无效输入事件，保持0%误报率，对运营商负担极小。仿真实验显示：能100%准确检测小至5%的需求扰动；在高达30%的遥测数据损坏情况下仍保持零误报；对现实级别的噪声、缺失或错误遥测数据维持接近零的误报率。

Conclusion: CrossCheck能够有效检测SDN控制器的无效输入，预防因控制基础设施漏洞导致的网络中断。系统在生产环境中证明了其实用性和准确性，能够在保持极低误报率的同时可靠检测各类无效输入，为WAN运营商提供了有效的故障预防工具。

Abstract: We present CrossCheck, a system that validates inputs to the Software-Defined Networking (SDN) controller in a Wide Area Network (WAN). By detecting incorrect inputs - often stemming from bugs in the SDN control infrastructure - CrossCheck alerts operators before they trigger network outages.
  Our analysis at a large-scale WAN operator identifies invalid inputs as a leading cause of major outages, and we show how CrossCheck would have prevented those incidents. We deployed CrossCheck as a shadow validation system for four weeks in a production WAN, during which it accurately detected the single incident of invalid inputs that occurred while sustaining a 0% false positive rate under normal operation, hence imposing little additional burden on operators. In addition, we show through simulation that CrossCheck reliably detects a wide range of invalid inputs (e.g., detecting demand perturbations as small as 5% with 100% accuracy) and maintains a near-zero false positive rate for realistic levels of noisy, missing, or buggy telemetry data (e.g., sustaining zero false positives with up to 30% of corrupted telemetry data).

</details>


### [134] [A Dual-AoI-based Approach for Optimal Transmission Scheduling in Wireless Monitoring Systems with Random Data Arrivals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06042)
*Yuchong Zhang,Yi Cao,Xianghui Cao*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文针对物联网无线监测系统，提出了一种基于双AoI模型的调度策略，通过MDP框架解决异步信息年龄演化问题，并推导出具有信道状态依赖阈值结构的低复杂度最优策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在物联网无线监测系统中，信息新鲜度（用信息年龄AoI量化）对实时监控和决策至关重要。然而，受限于信道资源稀缺、数据到达随机性及无线信道不可靠性等因素，传统仅依赖监控中心AoI的调度策略在异步AoI演化场景下效率低下。

Method: 提出双AoI模型以刻画传感器端和监控中心端的异步AoI动态；将问题建模为最小化长期时间平均AoI函数；基于马尔可夫决策过程（MDP）开发调度策略，分析确定性平稳最优策略的存在性和单调性；推导出具有信道状态依赖阈值结构的低复杂度调度策略。

Result: 证明了最优策略的确定性平稳性质及其单调性特征；建立了AoI目标稳定性的充要条件；仿真结果表明所提策略优于现有方法。

Conclusion: 双AoI模型能有效捕获异步信息年龄演化特性，所提出的低复杂度阈值结构调度策略在保证系统稳定性的同时显著降低了平均信息年龄，为物联网实时监测系统提供了高效的调度解决方案。

Abstract: In Internet of Things (IoTs), the freshness of system status information is crucial for real-time monitoring and decision-making. This paper studies the transmission scheduling problem in wireless monitoring systems, where information freshness -- typically quantified by the Age of Information (AoI) -- is heavily constrained by limited channel resources and influenced by factors such as the randomness of data arrivals and unreliable wireless channel. Such randomness leads to asynchronous AoI evolution at local sensors and the monitoring center, rendering conventional scheduling policies that rely solely on the monitoring center's AoI inefficient. To this end, we propose a dual-AoI model that captures asynchronous AoI dynamics and formulate the problem as minimizing a long-term time-average AoI function. We develop a scheduling policy based on Markov decision process (MDP) to solve the problem, and analyze the existence and monotonicity of a deterministic stationary optimal policy. Moreover, we derive a low-complexity scheduling policy which exhibits a channel-state-dependent threshold structure. In addition, we establish a necessary and sufficient condition for the stability of the AoI objective. Simulation results demonstrate that the proposed policy outperforms existing approaches.

</details>

### [135] [RoboLayout: Differentiable 3D Scene Generation for Embodied Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05522)
*Ali Shamsaddinlou*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了RoboLayout，一个面向具身智能体的室内场景布局生成框架，通过整合可达性约束和局部优化策略，生成既语义连贯又便于智能体交互的可行布局。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的视觉语言模型在从开放语言指令生成3D场景布局方面表现出色，但生成的布局往往缺乏对具身智能体交互可行性的考虑，特别是在物理受限的室内环境中，难以保证布局对智能体的可导航性和可操作性。

Method: 在LayoutVLM基础上提出RoboLayout框架：（1）将显式的可达性约束集成到可微分布局优化过程中；（2）引入通用的智能体抽象表示，支持服务机器人、仓储机器人、不同年龄段的人类或动物等多样化实体；（3）设计局部优化阶段，选择性重新优化问题物体放置位置，同时保持场景其他部分不变。

Result: 实验结果表明，RoboLayout在保持LayoutVLM强语义对齐和物理合理性的同时，显著提升了布局在智能体导航和操作方面的可行性；局部优化策略提高了收敛效率，无需增加全局优化迭代次数。

Conclusion: RoboLayout成功将智能体感知推理融入布局生成框架，实现了既符合语义约束又满足智能体物理能力的场景布局设计，为多样化的具身智能体环境定制提供了灵活的解决方案。

Abstract: Recent advances in vision language models (VLMs) have shown strong potential for spatial reasoning and 3D scene layout generation from open-ended language instructions. However, generating layouts that are not only semantically coherent but also feasible for interaction by embodied agents remains challenging, particularly in physically constrained indoor environments. In this paper, RoboLayout is introduced as an extension of LayoutVLM that augments the original framework with agent-aware reasoning and improved optimization stability. RoboLayout integrates explicit reachability constraints into a differentiable layout optimization process, enabling the generation of layouts that are navigable and actionable by embodied agents. Importantly, the agent abstraction is not limited to a specific robot platform and can represent diverse entities with distinct physical capabilities, such as service robots, warehouse robots, humans of different age groups, or animals, allowing environment design to be tailored to the intended agent. In addition, a local refinement stage is proposed that selectively reoptimizes problematic object placements while keeping the remainder of the scene fixed, improving convergence efficiency without increasing global optimization iterations. Overall, RoboLayout preserves the strong semantic alignment and physical plausibility of LayoutVLM while enhancing applicability to agent-centric indoor scene generation, as demonstrated by experimental results across diverse scene configurations.

</details>


### [136] [Real-Time AI Service Economy: A Framework for Agentic Computing Across the Continuum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05614)
*Lauri Lovén,Alaa Saleh,Reza Farahani,Ilir Murturi,Miguel Bordallo López,Praveen Kumar Donta,Schahram Dustdar*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究了设备-边缘-云连续体中实时AI服务的去中心化资源分配问题，发现服务依赖图的拓扑结构是价格稳定性的关键决定因素：层次化图结构（树或串并行）可实现稳定的价格均衡和高效分配，而复杂交叉依赖会导致价格振荡和管理困难。提出了混合管理架构，通过跨域集成器将复杂子图封装为资源切片，将价格波动降低70-75%而不牺牲吞吐量，使去中心化市场能够匹配集中式分配质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着实时AI服务在设备-边缘-云连续体中运行，自主AI代理生成延迟敏感的工作负载，编排多阶段处理管道，并在策略和治理约束下竞争共享资源。需要理解服务依赖图的结构如何影响去中心化、基于价格的资源分配机制在规模上的可靠性运行。

Method: 将服务依赖图建模为有向无环图(DAG)，节点表示计算阶段，边编码执行顺序；分析层次化结构（树或串并行）与复杂交叉依赖结构对价格收敛和分配效率的影响；提出混合管理架构，通过跨域集成器将复杂子图封装为资源切片；设计具有拟线性效用和离散切片项的机制；进行六组实验的系统消融研究（1,620次运行，每组10个种子）。

Result: 依赖图拓扑是价格稳定性和可扩展性的一阶决定因素；混合架构将价格波动降低70-75%而不牺牲吞吐量；治理约束产生可量化的效率-合规权衡，取决于拓扑和负载的联合作用；在真实出价下，去中心化市场匹配集中式价值最优基线，确认去中心化协调可复制集中式分配质量。

Conclusion: 服务依赖图的拓扑结构是去中心化资源分配机制能否可靠规模化运行的首要因素，层次化结构支持稳定的价格均衡和高效分配，而复杂依赖需要通过混合架构进行封装处理。通过适当的机制设计，去中心化协调可以实现与集中式分配相当的质量。

Abstract: Real-time AI services increasingly operate across the device-edge-cloud continuum, where autonomous AI agents generate latency-sensitive workloads, orchestrate multi-stage processing pipelines, and compete for shared resources under policy and governance constraints. This article shows that the structure of service-dependency graphs, modelled as DAGs whose nodes represent compute stages and whose edges encode execution ordering, is a primary determinant of whether decentralised, price-based resource allocation can work reliably at scale. When dependency graphs are hierarchical (tree or series-parallel), prices converge to stable equilibria, optimal allocations can be computed efficiently, and under appropriate mechanism design (with quasilinear utilities and discrete slice items), agents have no incentive to misreport their valuations within each decision epoch. When dependencies are more complex, with cross-cutting ties between pipeline stages, prices oscillate, allocation quality degrades, and the system becomes difficult to manage. To bridge this gap, we propose a hybrid management architecture in which cross-domain integrators encapsulate complex sub-graphs into resource slices that present a simpler, well-structured interface to the rest of the market. A systematic ablation study across six experiments (1,620 runs, 10 seeds each) confirms that (i) dependency-graph topology is a first-order determinant of price stability and scalability,(ii) the hybrid architecture reduces price volatility by up to 70-75% without sacrificing throughput, (iii) governance constraints create quantifiable efficiency-compliance trade-offs that depend jointly on topology and load, and (iv) under truthful bidding the decentralised market matches a centralised value-optimal baseline, confirming that decentralised coordination can replicate centralised allocation quality.

</details>


### [137] [Reasoning Models Struggle to Control their Chains of Thought](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05706)
*Chen Yueh-Han,Robert McCarthy,Bruce W. Lee,He He,Ian Kivlichan,Bowen Baker,Micah Carroll,Tomek Korbak*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文评估了推理模型控制其思维链（CoT）内容的能力（CoT可控性），发现模型对CoT的控制能力远低于对最终输出的控制能力，且受模型规模、强化学习训练量、测试时计算量和问题难度等因素影响。结果表明当前CoT可控性不太可能破坏CoT可监控性，但建议前沿实验室持续追踪未来模型中的这一能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 思维链监控是检测现代推理模型不当行为和理解其动机的有力工具。然而，如果模型能够控制其在CoT中表达的内容，就可能破坏CoT的可监控性。为了评估这种潜在风险，作者提出需要测量模型的CoT可控性，即模型在遵循CoT指令方面的能力。

Method: 引入CoT-Control评估套件，包含要求模型在解决问题时遵守特定CoT指令的任务（例如在讨论遗传学问题时不能使用'染色体'一词）。通过对比模型控制CoT和控制最终输出的成功率，评估CoT可控性。同时研究了模型规模、强化学习训练量、测试时计算量、问题难度、激励方式（直接请求vs间接激励）、提示词优化等因素对CoT可控性的影响。

Result: 推理模型的CoT可控性显著低于输出可控性，例如Claude Sonnet 4.5仅能在2.7%的情况下控制其CoT，但能以61.9%的成功率控制最终输出。较大模型的CoT可控性更高，而更多的强化学习训练、测试时计算量和更高的问题难度会降低可控性。即使给予模型逃避CoT监控的激励，可控性失败仍然存在；当告知模型正在被监控时，可控性略有提升。对抗性优化提示词并未显著提高可控性。

Conclusion: 当前CoT可控性不太可能成为CoT可监控性的失效模式，这让研究者保持谨慎乐观。然而，低可控性背后的机制尚不清楚。鉴于CoT可控性对维护CoT可监控性的重要性，建议前沿实验室在未来模型中持续追踪和监控CoT可控性指标。

Abstract: Chain-of-thought (CoT) monitoring is a promising tool for detecting misbehaviors and understanding the motivations of modern reasoning models. However, if models can control what they verbalize in their CoT, it could undermine CoT monitorability. To measure this undesirable capability -- CoT controllability -- we introduce the CoT-Control evaluation suite, which includes tasks that require models to solve problems while adhering to CoT instructions, e.g., reasoning about a genetics question without using the word 'chromosome'. We show that reasoning models possess significantly lower CoT controllability than output controllability; for instance, Claude Sonnet 4.5 can control its CoT only 2.7% of the time but 61.9% when controlling its final output. We also find that CoT controllability is higher for larger models and decreases with more RL training, test-time compute, and increased problem difficulty. CoT controllability failures extend even to situations in which models are given incentives (as opposed to direct requests) to evade CoT monitors, although models exhibit slightly higher controllability when they are told they are being monitored. Similarly, eliciting controllability by adversarially optimizing prompts does not meaningfully increase controllability. Our results leave us cautiously optimistic that CoT controllability is currently unlikely to be a failure mode of CoT monitorability. However, the mechanism behind low controllability is not well understood. Given its importance for maintaining CoT monitorability, we recommend that frontier labs track CoT controllability in future models.

</details>


### [138] [Evolving Medical Imaging Agents via Experience-driven Self-skill Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05860)
*Lin Fan,Pengyu Dai,Zhipeng Deng,Haolin Wang,Xun Gong,Yefeng Zheng,Yafei Ou*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出MACRO，一种自进化的医学智能体，能够从执行轨迹中自主发现并合成有效的多步骤工具序列为可复用的复合工具，从而实现工具集的动态扩展和自适应改进，在医学影像解释任务中显著提升了编排准确性和跨领域泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 临床影像解释本质上是多步骤、以工具为中心的过程，医生需要迭代地结合视觉证据与患者上下文来量化发现并优化决策。虽然基于LLM的智能体有望编排异构医疗工具，但现有系统将工具集和调用策略视为静态的，在现实世界的领域迁移、任务变化和诊断需求演进中表现脆弱，预定义的工具链经常退化且需要昂贵的手动重新设计。

Method: 提出MACRO（自进化、经验增强的医学智能体）：1）从验证的执行轨迹中自主识别重复出现的有效多步骤工具序列；2）将其合成为可复用的复合工具；3）注册为新的高级原语以持续扩展行为库；4）轻量级图像特征记忆将工具选择建立在视觉-临床上下文中；5）类GRPO训练循环强化对发现复合工具的可靠调用，实现最小监督下的闭环自我改进。

Result: 在多种医学影像数据集和任务上的大量实验表明，自主复合工具发现在多步骤编排准确性和跨领域泛化方面持续优于强基线和最新最先进的智能体方法，有效弥合了脆弱的静态工具使用与自适应、上下文感知的临床AI辅助之间的差距。

Conclusion: MACRO成功实现了从静态工具组合到经验驱动的工具发现的范式转变，通过自主发现和合成复合工具实现了智能体的自我进化，为临床AI辅助提供了更适应性强、上下文感知的解决方案，证明了自进化工具发现机制在医学影像分析中的有效性和实用价值。

Abstract: Clinical image interpretation is inherently multi-step and tool-centric: clinicians iteratively combine visual evidence with patient context, quantify findings, and refine their decisions through a sequence of specialized procedures. While LLM-based agents promise to orchestrate such heterogeneous medical tools, existing systems treat tool sets and invocation strategies as static after deployment. This design is brittle under real-world domain shifts, across tasks, and evolving diagnostic requirements, where predefined tool chains frequently degrade and demand costly manual re-design. We propose MACRO, a self-evolving, experience-augmented medical agent that shifts from static tool composition to experience-driven tool discovery. From verified execution trajectories, the agent autonomously identifies recurring effective multi-step tool sequences, synthesizes them into reusable composite tools, and registers these as new high-level primitives that continuously expand its behavioral repertoire. A lightweight image-feature memory grounds tool selection in a visual-clinical context, while a GRPO-like training loop reinforces reliable invocation of discovered composites, enabling closed-loop self-improvement with minimal supervision. Extensive experiments across diverse medical imaging datasets and tasks demonstrate that autonomous composite tool discovery consistently improves multi-step orchestration accuracy and cross-domain generalization over strong baselines and recent state-of-the-art agentic methods, bridging the gap between brittle static tool use and adaptive, context-aware clinical AI assistance. Code will be available upon acceptance.

</details>


### [139] [Conversational Demand Response: Bidirectional Aggregator-Prosumer Coordination through Agentic AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06217)
*Reda El Makroum,Sebastian Zwickl-Bernhard,Lukas Kranzl,Hans Auer*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了对话式需求响应（CDR）机制，利用代理式AI实现聚合商与产消者之间的双向自然语言交互，兼顾了自动化的可扩展性与用户决策的透明度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的住宅需求响应协调机制存在局限：全自动化方案缺乏透明度，而单向调度信号和价格警报无法支持用户进行知情决策，这限制了产消者的持续参与。

Method: 开发了一种双层多代理架构，包括负责分发灵活性请求的聚合商代理和评估可交付性与成本效益的产消者家庭能源管理系统（HEMS）代理；该系统支持双向自然语言交互，允许产消者主动向上游传递偏好变化。

Result: 概念验证评估表明，交互过程可在12秒内完成；该架构成功利用代理式AI弥合了聚合商与产消者之间的协调鸿沟。

Conclusion: CDR机制实现了自动化需求响应的可扩展性与持续参与所需的透明度、可解释性及用户自主性之间的平衡；所有系统组件已开源以促进复现和进一步开发。

Abstract: Residential demand response depends on sustained prosumer participation, yet existing coordination is either fully automated, or limited to one-way dispatch signals and price alerts that offer little possibility for informed decision-making. This paper introduces Conversational Demand Response (CDR), a coordination mechanism where aggregators and prosumers interact through bidirectional natural language, enabled through agentic AI. A two-tier multi-agent architecture is developed in which an aggregator agent dispatches flexibility requests and a prosumer Home Energy Management System (HEMS) assesses deliverability and cost-benefit by calling an optimization-based tool. CDR also enables prosumer-initiated upstream communication, where changes in preferences can reach the aggregator directly. Proof-of-concept evaluation shows that interactions complete in under 12 seconds. The architecture illustrates how agentic AI can bridge the aggregator-prosumer coordination gap, providing the scalability of automated DR while preserving the transparency, explainability, and user agency necessary for sustained prosumer participation. All system components, including agent prompts, orchestration logic, and simulation interfaces, are released as open source to enable reproducibility and further development.

</details>


### [140] [The World Won't Stay Still: Programmable Evolution for Agent Benchmarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05910)
*Guangrui Li,Yaochen Xie,Yi Liu,Ziwei Dong,Xingyuan Pan,Tianqi Zheng,Jason Choi,Michael J. Morais,Binit Jha,Shaunak Mishra,Bingrou Zhou,Chen Luo,Monica Xiao Cheng,Dawn Song*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出ProEvolve框架，通过图变换实现环境演化的可编程化，解决了现有基准测试假设静态环境、忽视现实世界动态性的问题，用于评估智能体对环境变化的适应能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能体基准测试大多假设静态环境（固定模式和工具集），忽视了现实世界的动态演化特性，无法有效评估智能体对环境变化的鲁棒性和适应能力。因此需要一种可扩展、可控的环境演化方法。

Method: 提出ProEvolve框架，核心是构建类型化关系图作为环境的统一显式表示，涵盖数据、工具和模式。通过图变换操作来表达环境能力的增删改，实现更新在工具、模式和数据访问间的协调传播。基于此实现：(1)将演化动态编程为图变换以自动生成环境；(2)通过子图采样和编程实例化任务沙盒。

Result: 成功将单个环境演化为200个环境和3000个任务沙盒，并对代表性智能体进行了基准测试，验证了框架的有效性和可扩展性。

Conclusion: ProEvolve提供了一种可编程、可扩展的环境演化方案，使智能体评估能够更好地反映现实世界的动态特性，为智能体鲁棒性评测提供了新的方法论支撑。

Abstract: LLM-powered agents fulfill user requests by interacting with environments, querying data, and invoking tools in a multi-turn process. Yet, most existing benchmarks assume static environments with fixed schemas and toolsets, neglecting the evolutionary nature of the real world and agents' robustness to environmental changes. In this paper, we study a crucial problem: how to evolve the agent environment in a scalable and controllable way, thereby better evaluating agents' adaptability to real-world dynamics. We propose ProEvolve, a graph-based framework that makes environment evolution programmable. At its core, a typed relational graph provides a unified, explicit representation of the environment: data, tools, and schema. Under this formalism, adding, removing, or modifying capabilities are expressed as graph transformations that coherently propagate updates across tools, schemas, and data access. Building on this, ProEvolve can (1) program the evolutionary dynamics as graph transformations to generate environments automatically, and (2) instantiate task sandboxes via subgraph sampling and programming. We validate ProEvolve by evolving a single environment into 200 environments and 3,000 task sandboxes, and benchmark representative agents accordingly.

</details>


### [141] [Talk Freely, Execute Strictly: Schema-Gated Agentic AI for Flexible and Reproducible Scientific Workflows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06394)
*Joel Strickland,Arjun Vijeta,Chris Moores,Oliwia Bodek,Bogdan Nenchev,Thomas Whitehead,Charles Phillips,Karl Tassenberg,Gareth Conduit,Ben Pellegrini*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文针对大语言模型（LLM）在科学工作流中缺乏确定性与可治理性的问题，提出"模式门控编排"原则，要求完整动作通过机器可检查的规范验证后方可执行。通过对20个系统的多模型评分分析，发现现有系统难以同时满足执行确定性与对话灵活性，并总结出三项操作原则以指导未来系统设计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型能够将研究者的自然语言目标转化为可执行计算，但科学工作流对确定性、溯源和治理有严格要求，而LLM在决定执行内容时难以保证这些特性，亟需一种平衡确定性执行与对话灵活性的解决方案。

Method: 对10个工业研发利益相关方的18位专家进行半结构化访谈，识别出确定性约束执行与对话灵活性两项竞争需求及边界属性。将需求操作化为执行确定性（ED）和对话灵活性（CF）两个维度，采用多模型协议（3个LLM家族的15个独立会话）对5个架构组的20个系统进行评分与审查。

Result: 多模型评分显示出实质到近乎完美的一致性（ED的Krippendorff α=0.80，CF的α=0.98），证明多模型LLM评分可作为人工专家面板的可复用替代方案。分析发现现有系统存在经验性帕累托前沿——没有系统能同时实现高灵活性与高确定性，但在生成式与工作流中心两种极端之间出现融合区域。

Conclusion: 提出模式门控架构，通过分离对话权限与执行权限来解耦确定性与灵活性之间的权衡，并提炼出三项操作原则：执行前澄清、约束的计划-行动编排、工具到工作流级别的门控，为系统采纳提供指导。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) can now translate a researcher's plain-language goal into executable computation, yet scientific workflows demand determinism, provenance, and governance that are difficult to guarantee when an LLM decides what runs. Semi-structured interviews with 18 experts across 10 industrial R&D stakeholders surface 2 competing requirements--deterministic, constrained execution and conversational flexibility without workflow rigidity--together with boundary properties (human-in-the-loop control and transparency) that any resolution must satisfy. We propose schema-gated orchestration as the resolving principle: the schema becomes a mandatory execution boundary at the composed-workflow level, so that nothing runs unless the complete action--including cross-step dependencies--validates against a machine-checkable specification.
  We operationalize the 2 requirements as execution determinism (ED) and conversational flexibility (CF), and use these axes to review 20 systems spanning 5 architectural groups along a validation-scope spectrum. Scores are assigned via a multi-model protocol--15 independent sessions across 3 LLM families--yielding substantial-to-near-perfect inter-model agreement (Krippendorff a=0.80 for ED and a=0.98 for CF), demonstrating that multi-model LLM scoring can serve as a reusable alternative to human expert panels for architectural assessment.
  The resulting landscape reveals an empirical Pareto front--no reviewed system achieves both high flexibility and high determinism--but a convergence zone emerges between the generative and workflow-centric extremes. We argue that a schema-gated architecture, separating conversational from execution authority, is positioned to decouple this trade-off, and distill 3 operational principles--clarification-before-execution, constrained plan-act orchestration, and tool-to-workflow-level gating--to guide adoption.

### [142] [DeepFact: Co-Evolving Benchmarks and Agents for Deep Research Factuality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05912)
*Yukun Huang,Leonardo F. R. Ribeiro,Momchil Hardalov,Bhuwan Dhingra,Markus Dreyer,Venkatesh Saligrama*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了AtS（Audit-then-Score）动态基准构建方法，通过审计-修正机制解决了深度研究报告（DRR）声明级事实验证的基准难题，并构建了DeepFact-Bench基准和DeepFact-Eval验证系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有事实验证器主要针对通用领域的事实型原子声明设计，缺乏适用于深度研究报告（DRR）声明级事实验证的基准；且静态专家标注基准在此场景下表现脆弱——博士级专家在未辅助情况下仅达到60.8%的准确率。

Method: 提出Evolving Benchmarking via Audit-then-Score (AtS)方法：当验证器与当前基准不一致时需提交证据，审计员裁决争议，接受的修订更新基准后再对模型评分。通过四轮AtS迭代，构建了可审计的版本化DRR事实验证基准DeepFact-Bench，并开发了文档级验证代理DeepFact-Eval（含分组轻量变体）。

Result: 专家在micro-gold集上的准确率从60.8%提升至90.9%，表明专家作为审计员比一次性标注者更可靠；DeepFact-Eval在DeepFact-Bench上优于现有验证器，且能良好迁移至外部事实验证数据集。

Conclusion: AtS动态基准方法有效解决了DRR事实验证基准的构建难题，专家审计机制显著提升标注质量，DeepFact-Eval为DRR事实验证提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Search-augmented LLM agents can produce deep research reports (DRRs), but verifying claim-level factuality remains challenging. Existing fact-checkers are primarily designed for general-domain, factoid-style atomic claims, and there is no benchmark to test whether such verifiers transfer to DRRs. Yet building such a benchmark is itself difficult. We first show that static expert-labeled benchmarks are brittle in this setting: in a controlled study with PhD-level specialists, unassisted experts achieve only 60.8% accuracy on a hidden micro-gold set of verifiable claims. We propose Evolving Benchmarking via Audit-then-Score (AtS), where benchmark labels and rationales are explicitly revisable: when a verifier disagrees with the current benchmark, it must submit evidence; an auditor adjudicates the dispute; and accepted revisions update the benchmark before models are scored. Across four AtS rounds, expert micro-gold accuracy rises to 90.9%, indicating experts are substantially more reliable as auditors than as one-shot labelers. We instantiate AtS as DeepFact-Bench, a versioned DRR factuality benchmark with auditable rationales, and DeepFact-Eval, a document-level verification agent (with a grouped lite variant) that outperforms existing verifiers on DeepFact-Bench and transfers well to external factuality datasets.
