### [144] [Agentic LLM Planning via Step-Wise PDDL Simulation: An Empirical Characterisation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06064)
*Kai Göbel,Pierrick Lorang,Patrik Zips,Tobias Glück*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文开发了PyPDDLEngine，一个将PDDL规划操作暴露为LLM工具调用的开源仿真引擎。在Blocksworld任务上，智能体式LLM规划相比直接规划仅提升3%（66.7% vs 63.7%），但成本高出5.7倍，且生成的计划比经典规划器更短，表明收益有限且可能源于训练数据回忆而非泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 任务规划是自主机器人系统的核心能力。尽管大语言模型（LLM）是否能作为可行的规划器与经典符号方法并肩仍是一个开放问题，但目前缺乏有效的工具来评估LLM在规划任务中的实际表现，特别是智能体式交互规划的有效性。

Method: 开发了PyPDDLEngine开源PDDL仿真引擎，通过模型上下文协议（MCP）接口将规划操作暴露为LLM工具调用。LLM作为交互式搜索策略，逐个选择动作、观察状态并可以重置重试。在102个IPC Blocksworld实例上评估四种方法：Fast Downward的两个变体作为经典基线、直接LLM规划（Claude Haiku 4.5）以及通过PyPDDLEngine的智能体式LLM规划，统一使用180秒时间预算。

Result: Fast Downward达到85.3%成功率。直接LLM和智能体式LLM分别达到63.7%和66.7%成功率，智能体式方法仅有3个百分点的适度优势，但每个解的token成本高出5.7倍。在大多数共同解决的难度块中，两种LLM方法生成的计划都比seq-sat-lama-2011更短，这与其迭代质量改进的结果一致，表明这是训练数据回忆而非泛化规划。

Conclusion: 智能体式LLM的收益取决于环境反馈的性质。代码智能体受益于编译器错误和测试失败等外部接地信号，而PDDL步骤反馈是自我评估的，智能体在没有外部验证的情况下评估自身进度。这说明在缺乏外部验证信号的规划任务中，智能体式方法的增益有限。

Abstract: Task planning, the problem of sequencing actions to reach a goal from an initial state, is a core capability requirement for autonomous robotic systems. Whether large language models (LLMs) can serve as viable planners alongside classical symbolic methods remains an open question. We present PyPDDLEngine, an open-source Planning Domain Definition Language (PDDL) simulation engine that exposes planning operations as LLM tool calls through a Model Context Protocol (MCP) interface. Rather than committing to a complete action sequence upfront, the LLM acts as an interactive search policy that selects one action at a time, observes each resulting state, and can reset and retry. We evaluate four approaches on 102 International Planning Competition (IPC) Blocksworld instances under a uniform 180-second budget: Fast Downward lama-first and seq-sat-lama-2011 as classical baselines, direct LLM planning (Claude Haiku 4.5), and agentic LLM planning via PyPDDLEngine. Fast Downward achieves 85.3% success. The direct and agentic LLM approaches achieve 63.7% and 66.7%, respectively, a consistent but modest three-percentage-point advantage for the agentic approach at $5.7\times$ higher token cost per solution. Across most co-solved difficulty blocks, both LLM approaches produce shorter plans than seq-sat-lama-2011 despite its iterative quality improvement, a result consistent with training-data recall rather than generalisable planning. These results suggest that agentic gains depend on the nature of environmental feedback. Coding agents benefit from externally grounded signals such as compiler errors and test failures, whereas PDDL step feedback is self-assessed, leaving the agent to evaluate its own progress without external verification.

</details>


### [145] [Aggregative Semantics for Quantitative Bipolar Argumentation Frameworks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06067)
*Yann Munro,Isabelle Bloch,Marie-Jeanne Lesot*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文在定量双极论证框架(QBAF)中提出了一种新的聚合语义家族，通过分别聚合攻击者和支持者并进行三阶段计算，实现了比模化解法更灵活、更具可解释性的渐进语义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的模化解法假设攻击者和支持者扮演对称角色，但在实际场景中二者往往具有非对称性。因此需要一种能够分别处理攻击者和支持者的新方法，以保持双极性特征并提供更强的参数化能力。

Method: 提出聚合语义家族，采用三阶段计算流程：首先为攻击者计算全局权重，其次为支持者计算全局权重，最后将这两个聚合值与论点的内在权重结合。该框架包含三个聚合函数，可根据具体场景选择满足不同性质的函数组合。

Result: 通过多个简单示例和最终的对比实验（测试了500种聚合语义），展示了聚合语义家族所能实现的行为范围及其优势。分解为三个可解释步骤的计算方式比现有方法更灵活且易于理解。

Conclusion: 聚合语义通过将计算分解为三个独立且可解释的步骤，在文献现有方法的基础上进一步保持了双极性特征，产生了更易理解且更具参数化能力的渐进语义，为处理攻击者和支持者非对称作用的场景提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Formal argumentation is being used increasingly in artificial intelligence as an effective and understandable way to model potentially conflicting pieces of information, called arguments, and identify so-called acceptable arguments depending on a chosen semantics. This paper deals with the specific context of Quantitative Bipolar Argumentation Frameworks (QBAF), where arguments have intrinsic weights and can attack or support each other. In this context, we introduce a novel family of gradual semantics, called aggregative semantics. In order to deal with situations in which attackers and supporters do not play a symmetric role, and in contrast to modular semantics, we propose to aggregate attackers and supporters separately. This leads to a three-stage computation, which consists in computing a global weight for attackers and another for supporters, before aggregating these two values with the intrinsic weight of the argument. We discuss the properties that the three aggregation functions should satisfy depending on the context, as well as their relationships with the classical principles for gradual semantics. This discussion is supported by various simple examples, as well as a final example on which five hundred aggregative semantics are tested and compared, illustrating the range of possible behaviours with aggregative semantics. Decomposing the computation into three distinct and interpretable steps leads to a more parametrisable computation: it keeps the bipolarity one step further than what is done in the literature, and it leads to more understandable gradual semantics.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种基于离线模型优化（MBO）的计算材料发现技术，将目标材料属性的直接优化融入生成过程；构建了领域专用模型CliqueFlowmer，该模型将基于小团体的MBO最新进展与Transformer和Flow生成技术相结合。

Abstract: Recent advances in deep learning inspired neural network-based approaches to computational materials discovery (CMD). Nevertheless, the increasingly popular generative modeling methods are ineffective at boldly exploring attractive regions of the materials space due to their maximum likelihood training. In this work, we offer an alternative CMD technique based on offline model-based optimization (MBO) that fuses direct optimization of a target material property into generation. To that end, we introduce a domain-specific model, dubbed CliqueFlowmer, that incorporates recent advances of clique-based MBO into transformer and flow generation. We validate CliqueFlowmer's optimization abilities and show that materials it produces strongly outperform those provided by generative baselines. To enable employment of CliqueFlowmer in specialized materials optimization problems and support interdisciplinary research, we open-source our code at https://github.com/znowu/CliqueFlowmer.

### [147] [Artificial Intelligence for Climate Adaptation: Reinforcement Learning for Climate Change-Resilient Transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06278)
*Miguel Costa,Arthur Vandervoort,Carolin Schmidt,João Miranda,Morten W. Petersen,Martin Drews,Karyn Morrisey,Francisco C. Pereira*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于强化学习的决策支持框架，用于长期洪水适应规划，以应对气候变化加剧的城市降雨洪水和交通系统中断问题。通过哥本哈根内城的案例研究（2024-2100年），该框架表现优于传统优化方法，能够发现协调的空间和时间适应路径，并学习影响减少与适应投资之间的权衡，从而制定更具韧性的策略。

Motivation: 气候变化预计将加剧降雨和由此产生的暴雨洪水，导致未来几十年城市交通系统中断增加。设计有效的适应策略具有挑战性，原因包括基础设施投资的长期性和序贯性、深度气候不确定性，以及洪水、基础设施和流动性影响之间的复杂相互作用。

Method: 提出了一种基于强化学习（RL）的决策支持框架，用于长期洪水适应规划。该框架被表述为一个综合评估模型（IAM），结合了降雨预测和洪水建模、交通模拟，以及对基础设施和流动性的直接和间接影响的量化。基于RL的方法学习适应策略，平衡投资和维护成本与避免的影响。

Result: 通过哥本哈根内城2024-2100年的案例研究评估了该框架，测试了多种适应选项和不同的信念及实现的气候情景。结果表明，该框架通过发现协调的空间和时间适应路径，并学习影响减少与适应投资之间的权衡，优于传统优化方法，产生了更具韧性的策略。

Conclusion: 研究展示了强化学习作为气候不确定性下适应性基础设施规划的灵活决策支持工具的潜力。

Abstract: Climate change is expected to intensify rainfall and, consequently, pluvial flooding, leading to increased disruptions in urban transportation systems over the coming decades. Designing effective adaptation strategies is challenging due to the long-term, sequential nature of infrastructure investments, deep climate uncertainty, and the complex interactions between flooding, infrastructure, and mobility impacts. In this work, we propose a novel decision-support framework using reinforcement learning (RL) for long-term flood adaptation planning. Formulated as an integrated assessment model (IAM), the framework combines rainfall projection and flood modeling, transport simulation, and quantification of direct and indirect impacts on infrastructure and mobility. Our RL-based approach learns adaptive strategies that balance investment and maintenance costs against avoided impacts. We evaluate the framework through a case study of Copenhagen's inner city over the 2024-2100 period, testing multiple adaptation options, and different belief and realized climate scenarios. Results show that the framework outperforms traditional optimization approaches by discovering coordinated spatial and temporal adaptation pathways and learning trade-offs between impact reduction and adaptation investment, yielding more resilient strategies. Overall, our results showcase the potential of reinforcement learning as a flexible decision-support tool for adaptive infrastructure planning under climate uncertainty.

</details>

*Giovanni Servedio,Potito Aghilar,Alessio Mattiace,Gianni Carmosino,Francesco Musicco,Gabriele Conte,Vito Walter Anelli,Tommaso Di Noia,Francesco Maria Donini*

Method: 提出EpisTwin神经符号框架，利用多模态语言模型将异构跨应用数据转化为语义三元组，构建可验证的用户中心化个人知识图谱。推理阶段，通过智能体协调器结合图谱检索增强生成（Graph RAG）与在线深度视觉细化，动态地将符号实体重新锚定到原始视觉上下文中进行复杂推理。同时引入PersonalQA-71-100合成基准测试来模拟真实用户数字足迹。

Result: EpisTwin在一组最先进的评判模型上展示了稳健的性能表现，证明了该方法的有效性。

Conclusion: EpisTwin为可信的个人AI提供了一个有前景的发展方向，通过神经符号推理和个人知识图谱实现了更全面、可靠的个人数据处理与推理能力。

Abstract: Personal Artificial Intelligence is currently hindered by the fragmentation of user data across isolated silos. While Retrieval-Augmented Generation offers a partial remedy, its reliance on unstructured vector similarity fails to capture the latent semantic topology and temporal dependencies essential for holistic sensemaking. We introduce EpisTwin, a neuro-symbolic framework that grounds generative reasoning in a verifiable, user-centric Personal Knowledge Graph. EpisTwin leverages Multimodal Language Models to lift heterogeneous, cross-application data into semantic triples. At inference, EpisTwin enables complex reasoning over the personal semantic graph via an agentic coordinator that combines Graph Retrieval-Augmented Generation with Online Deep Visual Refinement, dynamically re-grounding symbolic entities in their raw visual context. We also introduce PersonalQA-71-100, a synthetic benchmark designed to simulate a realistic user's digital footprint and evaluate EpisTwin performance. Our framework demonstrates robust results across a suite of state-of-the-art judge models, offering a promising direction for trustworthy Personal AI.

### [149] [SAHOO: Safeguarded Alignment for High-Order Optimization Objectives in Recursive Self-Improvement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06333)
*Subramanyam Sahoo,Aman Chadha,Vinija Jain,Divya Chaudhary*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了SAHOO框架，通过目标漂移指数、约束保持检查和回归风险量化三项机制，在递归自我改进过程中有效监控和对齐漂移，在代码生成和数学推理任务上分别获得18.3%和16.8%的性能提升，同时保持安全约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代AI系统已具备递归自我改进能力，但迭代式自我修改会导致微妙的对齐漂移风险，现有方法缺乏实用的监控和控制机制。

Method: 提出SAHOO框架，包含三个核心保障机制：(i)目标漂移指数(GDI)——结合语义、词汇、结构和分布测度的学习型多信号检测器；(ii)约束保持检查——强制执行语法正确性和非幻觉等安全关键不变量；(iii)回归风险量化——标记可能撤销先前收益的改进周期。

Result: 在代码生成、数学推理和真实性三个领域的189个任务上验证，代码任务提升18.3%，推理任务提升16.8%，约束在两个领域得到保持，真实性违规率维持低位。同时揭示了能力-对齐前沿：早期改进周期高效但后期对齐成本上升，以及流畅性与事实性等特定领域张力。

Conclusion: SAHOO框架使递归自我改进过程中的对齐保持变得可测量、可部署，并实现大规模系统性验证，为安全可控的自我改进系统提供了实用解决方案。

Abstract: Recursive self-improvement is moving from theory to practice: modern systems can critique, revise, and evaluate their own outputs, yet iterative self-modification risks subtle alignment drift. We introduce SAHOO, a practical framework to monitor and control drift through three safeguards: (i) the Goal Drift Index (GDI), a learned multi-signal detector combining semantic, lexical, structural, and distributional measures; (ii) constraint preservation checks that enforce safety-critical invariants such as syntactic correctness and non-hallucination; and (iii) regression-risk quantification to flag improvement cycles that undo prior gains. Across 189 tasks in code generation, mathematical reasoning, and truthfulness, SAHOO produces substantial quality gains, including 18.3 percent improvement in code tasks and 16.8 percent in reasoning, while preserving constraints in two domains and maintaining low violations in truthfulness. Thresholds are calibrated on a small validation set of 18 tasks across three cycles. We further map the capability-alignment frontier, showing efficient early improvement cycles but rising alignment costs later and exposing domain-specific tensions such as fluency versus factuality. SAHOO therefore makes alignment preservation during recursive self-improvement measurable, deployable, and systematically validated at scale.

### [150] [Boosting deep Reinforcement Learning using pretraining with Logical Options](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06565)
*Zihan Ye,Phil Chau,Raban Emunds,Jannis Blüml,Cedric Derstroff,Quentin Delfosse,Oleg Arenz,Kristian Kersting*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种混合分层强化学习方法（H²RL），通过两阶段框架将符号结构注入深度强化学习智能体，在保持深度策略表达能力的同时，利用逻辑选项预训练策略引导智能体避免短视奖励循环、学习目标导向行为，从而显著提升长视野决策能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度强化学习智能体常因过早过度利用早期奖励信号而导致目标错位。虽然已有符号方法通过编码稀疏目标和一致计划来解决此问题，但纯符号架构难以扩展至连续场景且复杂度高。

Method: 受人类技能习得能力的启发，提出一种两阶段混合框架：采用逻辑选项预训练策略，将符号结构注入神经网络强化学习智能体，引导学习策略远离短期奖励循环、转向目标导向行为，并允许最终策略通过标准环境交互进行精炼。

Result: 实验表明，该方法持续改进长视野决策能力，所训练的智能体在性能上优于强神经基线、符号基线及神经符号基线。

Conclusion: H²RL方法有效结合了符号方法与深度强化学习的优势，在不牺牲深度策略表达能力的条件下解决了奖励错位问题，为构建更鲁棒的长视野决策智能体提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Deep reinforcement learning agents are often misaligned, as they over-exploit early reward signals. Recently, several symbolic approaches have addressed these challenges by encoding sparse objectives along with aligned plans. However, purely symbolic architectures are complex to scale and difficult to apply to continuous settings. Hence, we propose a hybrid approach, inspired by humans' ability to acquire new skills. We use a two-stage framework that injects symbolic structure into neural-based reinforcement learning agents without sacrificing the expressivity of deep policies. Our method, called Hybrid Hierarchical RL (H^2RL), introduces a logical option-based pretraining strategy to steer the learning policy away from short-term reward loops and toward goal-directed behavior while allowing the final policy to be refined via standard environment interaction. Empirically, we show that this approach consistently improves long-horizon decision-making and yields agents that outperform strong neural, symbolic, and neuro-symbolic baselines.

</details>

### [151] [Why Ethereum Needs Fairness Mechanisms that Do Not Depend on Participant Altruism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05666)
*Patrick Spiesberger,Nils Henrik Beyer,Hannes Hartenstein*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文实证分析了以太坊中的利他主义区块提议者比例，发现真正符合去中心化和抗审查要求的提议者不足1.4%，远低于假设比例，表明仅依赖利他主义提议者的公平机制无法重建以太坊理想。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以太坊的去中心化和抗审查理想在实践中被削弱，现有公平机制提案依赖于足够比例的区块提议者遵守协议（即利他主义行为），但此前分析显示91%的提议者已将区块构建委托给中心化服务，需要对剩余提议者的真实行为进行评估。

Method: 对以太坊区块提议者进行实证分析，识别并量化与外部中心化服务交互的提议者比例，评估提议者是否表现出符合去中心化和抗审查目标的利他主义行为。

Result: 在看似利他的9%提议者中，另有6.1%也与外部服务交互；真正持续表现出利他主义行为的提议者不足1.4%，比例极低。

Conclusion: 仅依靠利他主义提议者的存在不足以确保公平机制重建以太坊的去中心化和抗审查理想，需要引入额外的激励或惩罚机制来保障协议目标的实现。

Abstract: Ethereum's ideals of decentralization and censorship resistance are undermined in practice, motivating ongoing efforts to reestablish these properties. Existing proposals for fairness mechanisms depend on the assumption that a sufficient fraction of block proposers adhere to Ethereum's protocols as intended. We refer to such proposers as altruistic, as this behavior may come at the cost of reduced revenue. Prior analyses indicate that a consistent share of 91 percent of proposers delegate block construction to centralized services, effectively signing externally constructed blocks blindly, and are thus not considered altruistic. To assess whether the remaining 9 percent of proposers genuinely exhibit altruistic behavior, we conducted an empirical analysis and found that an additional 6.1 percent also interact with such external services. Further, we found that less than 1.4 percent of proposers consistently acted in accordance with Ethereum's decentralization and censorship resistance objectives. These findings suggest that relying solely on the mere presence of altruistic proposers is insufficient to ensure that proposed fairness mechanisms reestablish Ethereum's ideals, highlighting the need for additional incentive- or penalty-based mechanisms.

</details>


### [152] [Parallelization Strategies for Dense LLM Deployment: Navigating Through Application-Specific Tradeoffs and Bottlenecks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05692)
*Burak Topcu,Musa Oguzhan Cim,Poovaiah Palangappa,Meena Arunachalam,Mahmut Taylan Kandemir*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文研究密集型大语言模型（Llama-3.1-70B和405B）的推理系统性能，通过分析输入特征、批处理和并行策略对延迟-吞吐量权衡的影响，发现张量并行(TP)有利于优化延迟目标，而流水线并行(PP)更适合吞吐量导向的应用，混合使用这两种策略可以有效控制延迟-吞吐量的相互影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着生成式AI和大语言模型应用的爆发式增长，密集型LLM因其强大的泛化能力、可扩展性、易于微调和多任务适应性而持续占据主导地位。在LLM推理系统中，延迟和吞吐量是核心性能指标，但两者存在内在耦合关系，优化其中一个往往会牺牲另一个。当模型参数超出设备内存容量时，批处理策略和并行配置会显著影响延迟和系统吞吐量，因此需要深入理解这些因素如何影响性能以满足服务等级协议(SLA)并维持推理质量。

Method: (1) 对两个代表性密集型LLM（Llama-3.1-70B和Llama-3.1-405B）的工作负载进行实证研究，重点关注节点内并行化方案；(2) 分析输入特征、批处理策略和并行策略如何影响延迟灵活性以及延迟-吞吐量权衡关系；(3) 识别关键性能瓶颈，为满足SLA和维持推理质量的设计选择提供指导。实验评估了张量并行(TP)、流水线并行(PP)及其混合配置在不同工作负载下的性能表现。

Result: 实证评估表明：张量并行(TP)能够改善延迟目标，更适合延迟敏感型应用；流水线并行(PP)更适合吞吐量导向的应用；通过控制TP和PP的度数进行混合使用，可以有效控制延迟-吞吐量之间的相互影响，为系统设计者提供了灵活的性能调优空间。研究还识别了影响系统性能的关键瓶颈因素。

Conclusion: 本研究为密集型LLM推理系统的设计与优化提供了重要见解：根据应用场景的延迟或吞吐量需求，可以选择合适的并行策略组合。TP适用于延迟敏感场景，PP适用于吞吐量优先场景，而混合策略则提供了精细控制延迟-吞吐量权衡的能力，帮助系统设计者在满足SLA要求的同时维持推理质量。

Abstract: Breakthroughs in the generative AI domain have fueled an explosion of large language model (LLM)-powered applications, whose workloads fundamentally consist of sequences of inferences through transformer architectures. Within this rapidly expanding ecosystem, dense LLMs--those that activate all model parameters for each token generation--form the foundation for advanced expert-based variants. Dense models continue to dominate because of their strong generalization ability, scalability, ease of fine-tuning, and versatility across diverse tasks. In LLM inference systems, performance is mainly characterized by latency, response time, and throughput (i.e., tokens generated per unit of time). Latency and throughput are inherently coupled: optimizing for one often comes at the expense of the other. Moreover, batching strategies and parallelism configurations, which are essential when dense model parameters exceed device memory capacity, can significantly affect both latency and overall system throughput. This paper (i) investigates the workloads of two representative dense LLMs--Llama-3.1-70B and Llama-3.1-405B, focusing in particular on intra-node parallelization schemes, (ii) analyzes how input characteristics, batching, and parallelism strategies influence latency flexibility and the latency-throughput tradeoff, and (iii) identifies key performance bottlenecks that inform design choices for meeting service-level agreements (SLAs) and sustaining inference quality. Our empirical evaluations reveal that Tensor Parallelism (TP) improves the latency objectives while Pipeline Parallelism (PP) is better-suited for throughput-oriented applications. We highlight that their hybrid usage by controlling the TP and PP degrees provides control over the latency-throughput interplay.

</details>


### [153] [A Lock-Free Work-Stealing Algorithm for Bulk Operations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05766)
*Raja Sai Nandhan Yadav Kataru,Danial Davarnia,Ali Jannesari*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对主从框架优化的无锁工作窃取队列，通过限制并发模型（单一所有者和单一窃取者）并支持批量操作，实现了恒定延迟的push性能，在批量操作场景下显著优于现有通用方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有无锁工作窃取算法面向通用并行运行时设计，在特定应用场景（如混合整数规划求解器的主从框架）中存在不必要的同步开销。针对这一限制，作者希望设计一个更高效的专用工作窃取队列。

Method: 设计了一种新的无锁工作窃取队列，针对最多一个所有者和一个并发窃取者的受限并发模型进行优化。该队列支持原生批量操作、无界增长，并通过轻量级同步机制减少开销。论文提供了线性化和无锁性质的informal证明。

Result: 基准测试表明，该队列的push操作保持恒定延迟，不随批量大小增长而增加（对比C++ Taskflow队列延迟急剧上升）；pop操作性能与其他实现相当；steal操作在不同窃取比例下延迟平稳；优化的steal变体可将延迟降低最多3倍。基于大图探索的伪工作负载测试显示所有实现均呈线性扩展。

Conclusion: 在受限并发模型下，专用设计的无锁工作窃取队列能够显著降低同步开销，在批量操作场景中性能优势明显。对于具有不规则节点处理时间的求解器工作负载，该算法的优势将进一步放大。

Abstract: Work-stealing is a widely used technique for balancing irregular parallel workloads, and most modern runtime systems adopt lock-free work-stealing deques to reduce contention and improve scalability. However, existing algorithms are designed for general-purpose parallel runtimes and often incur overheads that are unnecessary in specialized settings. In this paper, we present a new lock-free work-stealing queue tailored for a master-worker framework used in the parallelization of a mixed-integer programming optimization solver based on decision diagrams. Our design supports native bulk operations, grows without bounds, and assumes at most one owner and one concurrent stealer, thereby eliminating the need for heavy synchronization. We provide an informal sketch that our queue is linearizable and lock-free under this restricted concurrency model. Benchmarks demonstrate that our implementation achieves constant-latency push performance, remaining stable even as batch size increases, in contrast to existing queues from C++ Taskflow whose latencies grow sharply with batch size. Pop operations perform comparably across all implementations, while our steal operation maintains nearly flat latency across different steal proportions. We also explore an optimized steal variant that reduces latency by up to 3x in practice. Finally, a pseudo workload based on large-graph exploration confirms that all implementations scale linearly. However, we argue that solver workloads with irregular node processing times would further amplify the advantages of our algorithm.

</details>


### [154] [Gathering Autonomous Mobile Robots Under the Adversarial Defected View Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05788)
*Prakhar Shukla,Seshunadh Tanuj Peddinti,Subhash Bhagat*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文研究了对角线可视受限的移动机器人汇聚问题。在FSYNC模型下，解决(4,2)对角线视视图缺失问题；在ASYNC模型下，解决一般(N,K)对角线视视图缺失问题，均无需刚性运动假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有汇聚算法通常假设机器人具有完整感知能力，而在实际场景中，传感器故障可能导致机器人无法观测到所有其他机器人。针对这一缺陷，本文研究了对角线视视图缺失模型下的汇聚问题，其中被激活的机器人因感知故障仅能观测到部分机器人子集，且该子集由对抗者动态决定。

Method: 提出了两种分布式汇聚算法。对于FSYNC模型，设计了无需额外能力或坐标一致性的算法解决(4,2)对角线视视图缺失场景。对于ASYNC模型，在一维坐标轴方向和方向一致性的假设下，提出了适用于一般(N,K)对角线视视图缺失的算法。两种算法均不依赖刚性运动假设。

Result: 在FSYNC模型下，证明了(4,2)对角线视视图缺失环境下有限时间汇聚，解决了此前未解决的开放问题；在ASYNC模型下，建立了适用于任意1≤K<N-1的(N,K)对角线视视图缺失模型下的有限时间汇聚。两个结果均适用于非刚性运动场景。

Conclusion: 本研究首次在对抗性视视图缺失模型下实现了确定性有限时间汇聚，无需刚性运动假设。FSYNC模型下的结果填补了(4,2)案例的理论空白，ASYNC模型下的结果提供了更通用的解决方案。这些成果显著拓展了对故障容忍环境下分布式机器人协调能力的理解。

Abstract: This paper studies the gathering problem for a set of $N \ge 2$ autonomous mobile robots operating in the Euclidean plane under the distributed Look-Compute-Move model. We consider oblivious robots executing under the adversarial defected view model, in which an activated robot may observe only a restricted subset of robots due to adversarial visibility faults. Consequently, the information obtained during each Look phase may be incomplete and dynamically altered. The objective is to guarantee deterministic finite-time gathering at a location not known a priori despite such sensing restrictions. We present two distributed algorithms under distinct scheduling assumptions. In the fully synchronous (FSYNC) model, we prove finite-time gathering in the adversarial (4, 2) defected view setting, resolving a previously open case without requiring additional capabilities or coordinate agreement. In the asynchronous (ASYNC) model, we establish finite-time gathering under the general adversarial (N, K) defected view model, where an activated robot observes at most K of the other $N - 1$ robots for any $1 \le K < N - 1$. Both results hold under non-rigid motion. The proposed algorithm for the ASYNC model assumes agreement in the direction and orientation of one coordinate axis.

</details>

Abstract: Advances in multi-modal generative models are enabling new applications, from storytelling to automated media synthesis.   We tackle these challenges through the lens of real-time podcast video generation, integrating LLMs, text-to-speech, and video-audio generation. To meet tight SLOs, we design an adaptive, modular serving system, StreamWise, that dynamically manages quality (e.g., resolution, sharpness), model/content parallelism, and resource-aware scheduling. We leverage heterogeneous hardware to maximize responsiveness and efficiency. For example, the system can lower video resolution and allocate more resources to early scenes.

### [156] [Knowledge-driven Reasoning for Mobile Agentic AI: Concepts, Approaches, and Directions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05831)
*Guangyuan Liu,Changyuan Zhao,Yinqiu Liu,Dusit Niyato,Biplab Sikdar*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个知识驱动的推理框架，通过在带宽受限链路上同步可复用的决策知识并注入到设备端推理中，使资源受限的移动智能体在保持任务能力的同时降低延迟、能耗和错误累积。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 移动智能体平台（如边缘机器人和无人机）受SWAP-C约束和间歇性无线连接限制，现有方法主要优化单轮通信效率，但移动智能体需要在一连串任务中保持能力，缺乏跨任务知识复用机制。

Method: 提出DIKW启发的知识分类体系，将知识分为原始观测、情节级轨迹和持久跨任务知识，并进一步细分为检索型、结构化、程序化和参数化表示；通过从历史执行中提取可复用决策结构，在带宽受限链路上同步知识包，注入到设备端推理过程中。

Result: 发现知识暴露呈非单调性：过少会导致昂贵的试错重规划，过多则引入冲突线索和错误；在无人机案例研究中，紧凑的知识包使3B参数的机载模型实现了完美的任务可靠性，推理成本低于无知识设备端推理和云中心重规划方案。

Conclusion: 知识驱动的推理框架能够有效平衡推理加速与失败风险，在严格SWAP-C约束和间歇性连接环境下，使资源受限的移动智能体实现比传统方案更优的可靠性和效率。

Abstract: Mobile agentic AI is extending autonomous capabilities to resource-constrained platforms such as edge robots and unmanned aerial vehicles (UAVs), where strict size, weight, power, and cost (SWAP-C) constraints and intermittent wireless connectivity limit both on-device computation and cloud access. Existing approaches mostly optimize per-round communication efficiency, yet mobile agents must sustain competence across a stream of tasks. We propose a knowledge-driven reasoning framework that extracts reusable decision structures from past execution, synchronizes them over bandwidth-limited links, and injects them into on-device reasoning to reduce latency, energy, and error accumulation. A DIKW-inspired taxonomy distinguishes raw observations, episode-scoped traces, and persistent cross-task knowledge, and categorizes knowledge into retrieval, structured, procedural, and parametric representations, each with a distinct tradeoff between reasoning speedup and failure risk. A key finding is that knowledge exposure is non-monotonic: too little forces costly trial-and-error replanning, while too much introduces conflicting cues and errors. A UAV case study validates the framework, where a compact knowledge pack synchronized over intermittent backhaul enables a 3B-parameter onboard model to achieve perfect mission reliability with lower reasoning cost than both knowledge-free on-device reasoning and cloud-centric replanning.

</details>


### [157] [Domain-Adaptive Model Merging across Disconnected Modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05957)
*Junming Liu,Yusen Zhang,Rongchao Zhang,Wenkai Zhu,Tian Wu*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文提出了DMM，一种无需数据访问的模型合并框架，通过三步流程（独立训练、相似模型合并、基于合成伪数据的蒸馏优化）解决高度差异化模型的合并问题，在单模态和多模态任务上均取得了最优性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于隐私或异构性问题，跨域学习无法通过数据集中化来训练统一模型。模型合并提供了一种有吸引力的替代方案，避免了数据共享并降低了重训成本。然而，现有方法难以处理高度差异化的模型合并问题。

Method: DMM框架包含三个步骤：1）独立训练域特定模型；2）使用标准技术合并高相似度模型以保证稳定性；3）利用归一化统计信息合成伪数据，并通过这些样本引导轻量级优化，将差异化模型的知识蒸馏到合并模型中。

Result: 在单模态和多模态基准测试上的广泛实验表明，DMM相比现有合并方法取得了最优（SOTA）性能。该方法能有效保留罕见但关键的知识，同时保持稳定性。

Conclusion: DMM成功解决了高度差异化模型的无数据合并难题，通过合成伪数据和蒸馏优化实现了知识保留与稳定性的平衡，为跨域学习提供了有效的隐私保护解决方案。

Abstract: Learning across domains is challenging when data cannot be centralized due to privacy or heterogeneity, which limits the ability to train a single comprehensive model. Model merging provides an appealing alternative by consolidating knowledge from multiple specialized models into one, avoiding data sharing and reducing retraining cost. In this work, we present DMM, a data-free model merging framework designed to handle highly divergent models. DMM proceeds in three steps. First, domain-specific models are trained independently. Second, models with high similarity are merged using standard techniques to ensure stability. Third, we synthesize pseudo-data from normalization statistics and distill knowledge from divergent models into the merged model through a lightweight refinement guided by these samples. This approach preserves rare but critical knowledge while maintaining stability. Extensive experiments on unimodal and multimodal benchmarks show that DMM achieves state-of-the-art performance over existing merging methods.

</details>

These edge-deployed agents learn optimal charging strategies in real time based on local conditions and global policy updates. LegalEdge ensures low-latency decisions, high contract integrity, and efficient energy allocation. Our experimental results demonstrate significant improvements in learning convergence, transaction speed, and operational transparency, establishing LegalEdge as a scalable, intelligent, and accountable solution for next-generation EV charging networks.

### [159] [Provuse: Platform-Side Function Fusion for Performance and Efficiency in FaaS Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06170)
*Niklas Kowallik,Natalie Carl,Leon Pöllinger,Wei Wang,Sharan Santhahanam,David Bermbach*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文提出了Provuse，一种透明的平台端优化方案，通过在运行时自动融合独立部署的函数来消除冗余实例，从而解决了FaaS平台中函数调用时的双重计费问题，无需用户修改代码即可平均降低26.33%的端到端延迟和53.57%的内存使用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Function-as-a-Service (FaaS) 平台虽然提供了可扩展且成本高效的执行环境，但在包含多个函数的复杂应用中存在延迟增加和资源开销大的问题，特别是函数相互调用时产生的双重计费（double billing）问题，这导致了不必要的成本和性能损失。

Method: 提出了Provuse，一种透明的平台端优化方案，能够对独立部署的函数在运行时自动进行函数融合（function fusion），消除冗余的函数实例。该方法针对提供商管理的FaaS平台，利用其对函数入口点和部署构件的控制权，实现透明的运行时执行整合。作者基于tinyFaaS平台和Kubernetes提供了两种实现，证明了该方案与容器编排框架的兼容性。

Result: 实验评估表明，Provuse实现了显著的性能提升：平均端到端延迟降低26.33%，平均内存（RAM）使用量减少53.57%，并且在降低延迟和资源消耗方面表现一致。

Conclusion: 自动函数融合是一种有效的平台端策略，能够显著降低组合式FaaS应用的延迟和内存消耗，突显了无服务器系统中透明基础设施级优化的潜力，为FaaS平台优化提供了新的思路。

Abstract: Function-as-a-Service (FaaS) platforms provide scalable and cost-efficient execution but suffer from increased latency and resource overheads in complex applications comprising multiple functions, particularly due to double billing when functions call each other. This paper presents Provuse, a transparent, platform-side optimization that automatically performs function fusion at runtime for independently deployed functions, thereby eliminating redundant function instances. This approach reduces both cost and latency without requiring users to change any code. Provusetargets provider-managed FaaS platforms that retain control over function entry points and deployment artifacts, enabling transparent, runtime execution consolidation without developer intervention. We provide two implementations for this approach using the tinyFaaS platform as well as Kubernetes, demonstrating compatibility with container orchestration frameworks. An evaluation shows consistent improvements, achieving an average end-to-end latency reduction of 26.33% and a mean RAM usage reduction of 53.57%. These results indicate that automatic function fusion is an effective platform-side strategy for reducing latency and RAM consumption in composed FaaS applications, highlighting the potential of transparent infrastructure-level optimizations in serverless systems.

</details>


### [160] [MoEless: Efficient MoE LLM Serving via Serverless Computing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06350)
*Hanfei Yu,Bei Ouyang,Shwai He,Ang Li,Hao Wang*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文提出了MoEless，首个面向混合专家模型(LLM)的无服务器推理框架，通过轻量级负载预测和优化的专家扩展放置策略，解决了MoE模型中的专家负载不均衡问题，相比现有方案显著降低了推理延迟(43%)和成本(84%)。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代大语言模型普遍采用混合专家架构来降低训练成本并扩展模型规模，但MoE的稀疏激活机制导致严重的专家负载不均衡——少数专家过载而其他专家闲置，产生专家拖尾现象，增加了推理延迟和服务成本。现有的专家负载均衡方案假设静态资源配置，限制了专家的可扩展性和弹性，导致昂贵的实时专家交换或生成质量下降。

Method: 提出MoEless无服务器MoE服务框架：1) 设计轻量级、层级感知的预测器来准确估计即将到来的专家负载分布并主动识别拖尾专家；2) 设计优化的专家扩展和放置策略，最大化函数局部性，提高GPU利用率，平衡专家和GPU之间的负载；3) 基于Megatron-LM构建原型并在八GPU测试平台上部署。

Result: 在开源MoE模型和真实世界工作负载上的实验表明，与最先进的解决方案相比，MoEless将推理延迟降低了43%，推理成本降低了84%。

Conclusion: MoEless成功展示了无服务器架构在解决MoE模型专家负载不均衡问题上的有效性，通过动态资源调度和智能负载预测实现了显著的性能提升和成本节约，为大规模MoE模型的高效部署提供了新的技术路径。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have become a cornerstone of AI, driving progress across diverse domains such as content creation, search and recommendation systems, and AI-assisted workflows. To alleviate extreme training costs and advancing model scales, Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) has become a popular backbone for modern LLMs, which are commonly served in distributed deployment using expert parallelism (EP). However, MoE's sparse activation mechanism leads to severe expert load imbalance, where a few experts become overloaded while others remain idle, resulting in expert stragglers that inflate inference latency and serving cost. Existing expert load balancing solutions assume static resource configurations on serverful infrastructures, limiting expert scalability and elasticity, and resulting in either costly real-time expert swapping or degraded generation quality. We present MoEless, the first serverless MoE serving framework that mitigates expert load imbalance and accelerates inference via serverless experts. MoEless employs lightweight, layer-aware predictors to accurately estimate incoming expert load distributions and proactively identify stragglers. We design optimized expert scaling and placement strategies to maximize function locality, improve GPU utilization, and balance loads across experts and GPUs. MoEless is prototyped on top of Megatron-LM and deployed on an eight-GPU testbed. Experiments with open-source MoE models and real-world workloads show that MoEless reduces inference latency by 43% and inference cost by 84% compared to state-of-the-art solutions.

</details>


### [161] [Comparative Analysis of Cross-Chain Token Standards](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06388)
*Fatemeh Heidari Soureshjani,Jan Gorzny*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文对五种主流跨链代币标准（xERC20、OFT、NTT、CCT和SuperchainERC20）进行了全面的比较分析，探讨了它们在架构、消息传递机制、互操作性范围、链兼容性和安全特性等方面的技术设计与差异化特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 跨链代币标准实现了在多个区块链上存在的统一总供应模型的可替代代币，但不同的标准和框架在实现方法、信任模型和目标生态系统方面存在显著差异，因此有必要对这些标准进行系统的比较分析。

Method: 对五种主流跨链代币标准和框架进行全面比较分析：xERC20标准（实现ERC-7281）、Omnichain Fungible Token (OFT)标准、Native Token Transfers (NTT)框架、Cross-Chain Token (CCT)标准以及SuperchainERC20标准（实现ERC-7802）。考察每个标准的独特属性和技术设计，包括架构、消息传递机制、互操作性范围、链兼容性和安全特性。

Result: 分析表明，虽然所有这些标准都致力于实现无缝的跨链可替代性，但它们在实现方法、信任模型和目标生态系统方面存在显著差异。

Conclusion: 不同跨链代币标准在追求统一目标的过程中采用了差异化的技术路径，开发者和项目方需要根据具体的应用场景、生态系统需求和安全考量选择合适的跨链代币标准。

Abstract: Cross-chain token standards enable fungible tokens that exist across multiple blockchains with a unified total supply model. This paper presents a comprehensive comparative analysis of five leading cross-chain token standards and frameworks: the xERC20 standard (implementing ERC-7281), the Omnichain Fungible Token (OFT) standard, the Native Token Transfers (NTT) framework, the Cross-Chain Token (CCT) standard, and the SuperchainERC20 standard (implementing ERC-7802). We examine each standard's distinguishing properties and technical design, including architecture, message-passing mechanisms, interoperability scope, chain compatibility, and security features. Our analysis reveals that while all these standards share the goal of seamless cross-chain fungibility, they differ significantly in implementation approach, trust model, and target ecosystem.

</details>
